- define the weaker Paper-17 export boundary:
  `HK-X15-CLOSE + HK-PROJ-CLOSE + HK-REG-CLOSE` gives only a
  regulator-independent projective positive `X_15` tower, while full
  `CYM_WL` still requires RP/covariance transport, loop continuity,
  nontriviality, and whole-process compatibility;
- reduce reflection positivity and Euclidean covariance to summable finite
  OS and Euclidean-motion approximant defects by proving
  `HK-RPCOV-CLOSE => AYM-RP-COV`;
- split off the reflection-positivity half first: exact heat-kernel cutoff
  RP plus symmetric-positive scalar counterterms/readouts gives
  `symmetric-positive OS readout + HK-RP-LEDGER
  => RP half of HK-RPCOV-CLOSE`; the remaining RP burden is summable
  counterterm, binning, projectivity, regulator/chart, and volume defects;
- split off the Euclidean covariance half next: define `Euc_adm` as exact
  hypercubic symmetries plus continuum motions represented by declared loop
  approximants, then prove
  `Euc_adm + Euclidean-invariant counterterm/readout ledger + HK-COV-LEDGER
  => covariance half of HK-RPCOV-CLOSE`;
- assemble
  `HK-RP-LEDGER + HK-COV-LEDGER => HK-RPCOV-CLOSE => AYM-RP-COV`,
  with exact cutoff defects for hypercubic symmetries and summable
  approximant/transport defects for continuum motions;
- reduce loop completion to a transported Paper-12 Wilson-loop continuity
  modulus: use the admissible loop metric, calibrated perimeter/cusp
  counterterms, product smearing-removal, and AF loop-variation estimate;
  split the transport defect into Paper-12 tail, lattice/block approximant,
  binning, perimeter, cusp, smearing, projective, regulator/chart, and
  finite-volume losses; prove
  `Paper-12 loop package + HK-LC-TRANSPORT => HK-LC-CLOSE => AYM-LC`;
- reduce nontriviality to a scalar anchor extracted from the Paper-13/15
  Creutz route: import either the Paper-13 scale-resolved Creutz margin
  `kappa_res c_0` or the Paper-15 explicit reserve `M_15^{bd}>0`, convert it
  to a seed scalar-loop reserve `c_seed`, then split final transport losses
  into Creutz/surface/decoration, scalar extraction, loop approximant,
  finite-battery/binning, counterterm, loop-continuity, projective,
  regulator/chart, and finite-volume losses; prove
  `Paper-13/15 anchor package + HK-NT-TRANSPORT => HK-NT-CLOSE => AYM-NT`;
- reduce whole-process compatibility to a common-tower ledger audit: fix one
  cofinal family `i=(a_i,L_i,beta_i,B_i,Rep_i,Loop_i)`, one pushed-forward
  law `Gamma_i`, one battery/readout ledger, one family of restriction and
  regulator/chart maps, one loop-approximant ledger, one counterterm branch
  ledger, and one constants ledger; add the no-hidden-divisibility clause,
  forbidding unrecorded partial-kernel composition; prove
  `HK-WP-CLOSE => AYM-WP`;
- assemble the heat-kernel route as
  `HK-CYC-CLOSE => AYM-CLOSE => strong CYC => CYM_WL`, where
  `HK-CYC-CLOSE` is the conjunction of `HK-X15-CLOSE`, `HK-PROJ-CLOSE`, `HK-REG-CLOSE`,
  `HK-RPCOV-CLOSE`, `HK-LC-CLOSE`, `HK-NT-CLOSE`, and `HK-WP-CLOSE`;
- add a compact gate ledger distinguishing proved reductions, conditional
  analytic gates, and still-open continuum closure gates;
- prove the finite-cutoff record-law part directly for standard
  reflection-positive lattice actions, then prove
  `AYM-CLOSE => verified positive nCPSC => positive X_15 tower => strong CYC`;
- state exactly which nonperturbative input has been proved, imported, or left
  conditional.

Pass condition:

- a nontrivial reflection-positive Euclidean-covariant continuum
  `SU(N)` Wilson-loop functional obtained from the ISP whole-process record
  ledger. In the Paper-16 notation, verified positive `nCPSC` plus strong
  `CYC` gives `CYM_WL`; equivalently, the actual-trajectory certificate
  `AYM-CLOSE` gives `CYM_WL`.

Fail condition:

- one or more Paper-14/15 gates remain conditional, so the result is a
  conditional continuum-Yang-Mills reconstruction theorem rather than a full
  construction. The sharp obstruction types are `FBE`, `AFRCE`, KP entropy,
  character tail, surface reserve, Creutz reserve, projectivity,
  RP/covariance, loop completion, triviality, or whole-process
  compatibility. After Paper 16, these are packaged as failure modes of
  `AYM-CLOSE` on the actual asymptotically-free `4D SU(N)` trajectory.

## V3 Paper 17: Mass Gap Program

Suggested title:

`Mass Gap Gates For Relativistic ISP Yang-Mills`

Draft:

`relativistic-isp-v3-paper17-yang-mills-mass-gap-gates.md`

Main question:

> Can the continuum-facing ISP Yang-Mills functional support a positive
> spectral gap?

Main job:

- define gauge-invariant glueball or field-strength correlators as operational
  record observables;
- prove exponential clustering with a positive continuum mass scale;
- use reflection positivity to convert Euclidean clustering into a spectral
  gap;
- separate true mass gap from smearing, finite-volume, and battery artifacts.

Initial gate structure:

- import `CYM_WL` from Paper 16, not a primitive Hilbert-space theory;
- define operational gauge-invariant mass-gap probes `MG-OBS` from closed
  Wilson-loop records and centered OS vectors;
- reconstruct the gauge-invariant OS sector through `MG-OS-CLOSE`: reflection
  positivity, Euclidean covariance, null-space invariance, and OS-norm
  continuity of time translations imply a strongly continuous OS semigroup;
- prove the spectral theorem
  `MG-EXP(m) + MG-OBS + MG-OS => MGAP(m)`;
- reduce `MG-EXP-CLOSE` through the Paper-13--15 connected-polymer route:
  Paper-14 `FBE`, Paper-15 positive `nCPSC/X_15`, the Paper-13
  connected-cumulant KP criterion, and a marked two-point extension
  `MG-2PT-KP` over the mass-gap probe batteries;
- first concrete battery: `G_box`, the centered plaquette/clover scalar
  loop records and degree-two products in one block collar;
- first finite-battery certificate:
  `CYM_WL + finite-battery MG-OBS(G_box) + MG-WP + BOX-2PT-KP + BOX-MASS
  => MG-EXP-CLOSE(m_phys,box) on G_box`;
- cofinal battery sequence: nested finite loop/product batteries `G_j`
  built from the Paper-13 dense loop skeleton, Paper-12 finite-battery
  renormalized loop records, increasing representation sets, larger boxes,
  and increasing product degree;
- cofinal marked-KP certificate:
  `G_j-2PT-KP` for every `j`, with constants
  `mu_j,h_j,lambda_mark,j,m_j,ell_j,Delta_tot,j`;
- uniform reserve gate:
  `MG-UNIF(m_*)`, meaning
  `inf_j [m_j/ell_j - Delta_tot,j] >= m_*>0`;
- constants-degradation ledger:
  track `mu_j`, `h_j`, `lambda_mark,j`, `ell_j`, and all pieces of
  `Delta_tot,j`; a simple sufficient test is uniform lower decay, uniform
  entropy/marking bounds, bounded block scale, and bounded total rate loss;
- dense-sector clustering theorem:
  `cofinal MG-OBS + G_j-2PT-KP for all j + MG-UNIF(m_*) + MG-WP
  => MG-EXP-CLOSE(m_*)`;
- direct mass-gap closure theorem:
  `CYM_WL + MG-OS + MG-WP + cofinal MG-OBS + G_j-2PT-KP for all j
  + MG-UNIF(m_*) => MGAP(m_*)`;
- export the raw rate `m_raw=m_KP/ell_blk` and require the visible reserve
  `m_KP/ell_blk > Delta_tot`;
- debit finite-volume, cutoff, smearing, block-scale, finite-battery,
  regulator/chart, and projective losses through `MG-ART`;
- enforce whole-process compatibility through `MG-WP`;
- assemble
  `CYM_WL + MG-OBS + MG-OS + G_j-2PT-KP + MG-UNIF(m_*) + MG-WP
  => MG-CLOSE(m_*) => MGAP(m_*)`.

Pass condition:

- a positive lower spectral gap for a declared gauge-invariant sector.

Fail condition:

- only finite-volume or smeared correlation-length bounds are obtained, or
  the marked two-point/cofinal extension of the Paper-13--15 KP package
  fails, or the debited mass inequality loses its positive reserve, or the
  first-battery result cannot be extended to a cofinal dense probe family;
- each finite `G_j` clusters, but the uniform reserve fails:
  `inf_j [m_j/ell_j - Delta_tot,j]=0`.

## V3 Paper 18: Confinement Program

Suggested title:

`Confinement, Uniform Marked KP, And 4D Gauge-Theory Completion Gates`

Draft:

`relativistic-isp-v3-paper18-confinement-area-law-isp-yang-mills.md`

Main question:

> Can ISP Yang-Mills prove confinement or area-law estimates strong enough to
> close the Paper-17 mass-gap gates and turn the V3 construction into a
> mathematically complete four-dimensional quantum gauge-theory example?

Main job:

- enforce the ontology guardrail: surfaces, sheets, polymers, flux tubes,
  charged endpoints, and gauge charts are allowed only as auxiliary
  bookkeeping that is eliminated into scalar record inequalities;
- define the confinement observables: rectangular Wilson loops, Creutz
  ratios, Polyakov-loop correlators, and static-potential records;
- declare the confinement record domain `CONF-REC`, so loop records,
  Creutz domains, and charged boundary instruments are typed before any
  confinement estimate is used;
- reduce `CONF-REC` to imported gates:
  `CYM_WL + Paper-12 renormalization + MG-WP + CR-DOM^cof + CH-BDY`;
- reduce `CR-DOM` through finite-window Creutz legalization:
  `CR-POS(J,kappa_CR,J) + CR-LCONT(J,kappa_CR,J) => CR-FIN + CR-CONT
  => CR-DOM(J,kappa_CR,J)`, and then cofinally `CR-DOM^cof`;
- prove `CR-POS` through the positive-main-term dominance ledger `CR-MTD`:
  a positive source `P_alpha,J` dominates sheet, volume, cutoff,
  counterterm, regulator, and projective errors;
- prove `CR-LCONT` through the loop-continuity modulus ledger `CR-LMOD`:
  Paper-16 loop continuity plus Paper-12 renormalization, volume,
  regulator, and projective moduli stay below `kappa_CR,J`;
- reduce the first-battery Creutz confinement input:
  `CR-MTD_box(sigma,delta_box,kappa_CR,box) + CR-LMOD_box(delta_box,kappa_CR,box)`
  plus positive counterterms implies `CONF-CR_box(sigma)`, where
  `CR-MTD_box` supplies the finite-stage Creutz-ratio main-term reserve and
  `CR-LMOD_box` transports that reserve through the continuum log-ratio
  modulus;
- reduce `CR-MTD_box` through the Paper-15 positive Creutz reserve:
  `P15-CR-RES_box + CR-ERR_box(delta_box) + S_15,box >= (sigma+2 delta_box)s_0^2`
  proves `CR-MTD_box`, where
  `S_15,box=gamma_15,box M_15^{bd}-epsilon_15_to_box`, and
  `CR-ERR_box` explicitly budgets sheet, volume, cutoff, counterterm,
  regulator, projective, battery, and log-normalization errors without
  double-counting `Delta_dec^{bd}` or `T_loss^{bd}`;
- package the Paper-15 first-battery Creutz route as
  `P15-CREUTZ-PASS_box`, bundling the generic Creutz positivity ledger,
  `P15-CR-RES_box`, `CR-ERR_box`, `CR-LMOD_box`, positive
  Paper-12/Paper-16 counterterms, and
  `S_15,box >= (sigma+2 delta_box)s_0^2`, then prove
  `P15-CREUTZ-PASS_box => CONF-CR_box(sigma)`;
- prove the upstream positivity-window theorem:
  with
  `delta_req,box=max(E_box^*/s_0^2,
  4 omega_box^*/(kappa_CR,box s_0^2))`, if
  `S_15,box>2 delta_req,box s_0^2`, then there are admissible
  `delta_box` and `sigma>0` for the Paper-15 Creutz pass;
- reduce `CR-LMOD_box` itself by a first-battery log-Lipschitz theorem:
  if finite-stage and continuum loop expectations in every Creutz slot are
  bounded below by `kappa_CR,box`, and
  `4 omega_CR,box(alpha)/kappa_CR,box <= delta_box s_0^2`, then the
  induced Creutz log-ratio modulus is at most `delta_box s_0^2`;
- package the quantitative loop-modulus pass
  `CR-LMOD-QUANT_box => CR-LMOD_box`, importing Paper-16 `HK-LC-CLOSE`,
  the four-slot lower bound, and the explicit
  `omega_CR,box` inequality;
- specify `CH-BDY` by finite-regulator charged-boundary protocols:
  representation, boundary worldlines or Polyakov lines, scalar closure,
  positive boundary counterterms, projective compatibility, and static-rate
  extraction;
- prove a renormalized area-law or equivalent confinement certificate with
  positive string tension `sigma>0` after perimeter/cusp and loop-continuity
  renormalization;
- prove the marked bridge gates `CONF-MARK_j(sigma)` by the concrete
  `AL2MARK_j` transfer package: endpoint closure, area comparison,
  counterterm cancellation, Creutz tiling fallback, endpoint locality, and
  record compatibility;
- reduce `AL2MARK_j` to two checkable ledgers:
  `MARK-GEOM_j` for closure geometry and area comparison, and
  `MARK-LOSS_j` for endpoint collars, counterterms, tiling, and bounded
  area defects;
- prove the first-battery geometry half under the standard block-face hull
  convention:
  `G_box` plaquette-clover hulls imply `MARK-GEOM_box` with
  `N_cl,box=1`, `c_geom,box=alpha_box s_0`, and finite `b_area,box`;
- prove the first-battery loss half under same-ledger finite local bounds:
  endpoint collar factors are amplitude-only, bounded area defects are
  amplitude-only, `epsilon_ctr,box=log M_ctr,box`, and
  `epsilon_tile,box=log M_tile,box`;
- prove the first-battery marked bridge:
  `MARK-GEOM_box + MARK-LOSS_box + CONF-AL or CONF-CR
  => AL2MARK_box => CONF-MARK_box`;
- import the first-battery marked KP gate from earlier papers:
  `BOX-MSKP-IMPORT := Paper-14 FBE_box + Paper-15 positive nCPSC_box`
  after endpoint enlargement to `G_box`, plus the Paper-17 endpoint-marking
  ledger, and prove `BOX-MSKP-IMPORT => MS-KP_box`;
- publish the imported first-battery KP constants:
  `A_box^S`, `C_cum,box^S`, `h_box^S`, `r_box^S`,
  `eta_ch,box`, `lambda_mark,box^S`, `c_box^S(O,P)`, and
  `B_box(O,P)`;
- publish the compact first-battery constants ledger:
  `alpha_box`, `s_0`, `sigma`, `M_ctr,box`, `M_tile,box`,
  `A_box^S`, `C_cum,box^S`, `eta_ch,box`, `h_box^S`,
  `lambda_mark,box^S`, `D_KP,box`, `R_clean,box`, and
  `R_Creutz,box`;
- define the branch reserve certificates `BOX-RESERVE-PASS(clean)` and
  `BOX-RESERVE-PASS(Creutz)`, and prove
  `BOX-RESERVE-PASS(beta) => BOX-CONF-PASS`;
- prove the Paper-15 Creutz branch export:
  `P15-CREUTZ-PASS_box + BOX-MSKP-IMPORT + MARK-GEOM_box + MARK-LOSS_box
  + R_Creutz,box > D_KP,box => BOX-RESERVE-PASS(Creutz)`;
- prove the single-window Creutz closing inequality:
  with `L_Creutz,box=log M_ctr,box+log M_tile,box+h_box^S+lambda_mark,box^S`,
  the condition
  `alpha_box(S_15,box-2 delta_box s_0^2)>L_Creutz,box+D_KP,box`
  gives one `sigma` satisfying both the upstream Paper-15 extraction reserve
  and the downstream marked-KP reserve;
- prove the clean first-battery pass theorem:
  direct `CONF-AL(sigma)` plus `G_box` block-face hulls, same-counterterm
  local loss bounds, `BOX-MSKP-IMPORT => MS-KP_box`, and
  `R_clean,box > D_KP,box` imply `BOX-CONF-PASS`, where
  `R_clean,box=alpha_box sigma s_0^2-h_box^S-lambda_mark,box^S`;
- prove the Creutz fallback first-battery pass theorem:
  `CONF-CR(sigma)` plus the same geometry/loss inputs,
  `BOX-MSKP-IMPORT => MS-KP_box`, and
  `R_Creutz,box > D_KP,box` imply `BOX-CONF-PASS`, where
  `R_Creutz,box=alpha_box sigma s_0^2-log M_ctr,box-log M_tile,box-h_box^S-lambda_mark,box^S`;
- package the branch worksheet:
  available branch set `A_box^branch`, best available reserve
  `R_best,box=max_beta R_beta,box`, and pass/fail test
  `R_best,box>D_KP,box`, now routed through `BOX-RESERVE-PASS(beta)`;
- prove the Paper-15 Creutz clustering specialization:
  `P15-CREUTZ-PASS_box + BOX-MSKP-IMPORT + MARK-GEOM_box
  + MARK-LOSS_box + R_Creutz,box > D_KP,box + BOX-MASS
  => MG-EXP-CLOSE(m_phys,box) on G_box`;
- make `BOX-MASS` numerical:
  define `G_box^beta=R_box^beta-D_KP,box`; if
  `G_box^beta>s_0 Delta_tot,box`, choose
  `m_box=(G_box^beta+s_0 Delta_tot,box)/2` and export
  `m_phys,box=(G_box^beta-s_0 Delta_tot,box)/(2s_0)>0`;
- publish the `CONF-MARK_j` constants ledger:
  `sigma`, `kappa_CR`, `s_0`, `c_geom,j`, `b_area,j`,
  `epsilon_area0,j`, `epsilon_area,j`, `h_j^S`, `lambda_mark,j^S`,
  `ell_j`, `Delta_conf,j`, and `B_j(O,P)`;
- prove the first-battery bridge:
  `BOX-CONF-PASS => BOX-2PT-KP`, and with Paper 17 `BOX-MASS`,
  `BOX-CONF-PASS + BOX-MASS => MG-EXP-CLOSE(m_phys,box)` on `G_box`;
- prove the explicit reserve-to-clustering corollary:
  `R_beta,box>D_KP,box` for an available branch, plus `BOX-MASS` for a
  selected `m_box` below the reserve surplus, implies
  `MG-EXP-CLOSE(m_phys,box)` on `G_box`;
- cofinalize the bridge by proving
  `G_j-CONF-PASS => G_j-2PT-KP` for every cofinal battery;
- define and use the true cofinal completion gate
  `CONF-COFINAL-PASS(m_*)`, requiring selected exported rates `m_j` with
  `inf_j [m_j/ell_j - Delta_conf,j] >= m_*>0`;
- define the cofinal Paper-15 Creutz program
  `COF-P15-CREUTZ(m_*)`: for every cofinal battery, prove the `j`-level
  Paper-15 Creutz pass, marked geometry/loss, marked KP stability, and the
  uniform surplus
  `inf_j [G_j^Creutz/ell_j - Delta_conf,j] >= 2m_* > 0`;
- prove
  `COF-P15-CREUTZ(m_*) => CONF-COFINAL-PASS(m_*) => MGAP(m_*)`;
- define the actual-trajectory confinement certificate
  `AYM-CONF-CLOSE(m_*)`, requiring the actual `4D SU(N)` continuum record
  law to verify the cofinal Paper-15 Creutz program with quantitative
  denominators, loop-modulus control, single-window Creutz closing
  inequalities, marked bridge stability, and the uniform Paper-17 rate
  surplus on one whole-process ledger;
- split `AYM-CONF-CLOSE` into the eight workbench subcertificates:
  `AYM-CONF-LAW`, `AYM-CONF-WIN`, `AYM-CONF-RES`, `AYM-CONF-LMOD`,
  `AYM-CONF-SWIN`, `AYM-CONF-MARK`, `AYM-CONF-RATE`, and `AYM-CONF-WP`;
- map those subcertificates to existing V3 gates:
  `HK-CYC-CLOSE`, `HK-X15-CLOSE`, `HK-CREUTZ-CLOSE`, `HK-LC-CLOSE`,
  `MARK-GEOM_j`, `MARK-LOSS_j`, `MS-KP_j`, `COF-BRANCH-SURP`,
  `HK-WP-CLOSE`, `MG-WP`, and `CONF-WP`;
- prove/import cofinal `S_15,j` positivity by the calibration gate
  `P15-RES-CAL_j`: Paper 16 `HK-CREUTZ-CLOSE_j` exports
  `M_15,j^bd>0`, the scalar readout calibration has `gamma_15,j>0`, and
  `epsilon_15_to_j<gamma_15,j M_15,j^bd`, hence
  `S_15,j=gamma_15,j M_15,j^bd-epsilon_15_to_j>0` for every cofinal `j`;
- reduce the cofinal loop-modulus debit to the explicit inequality
  `delta_req,j<S_15,j/(2 ell_j^2)`, with
  `delta_req,j=max(E_j^*/ell_j^2,4 omega_j^*/(kappa_CR,j ell_j^2))`;
- reduce the cofinal single-window step to the nonempty interval condition
  `alpha_j(S_15,j-2 delta_j ell_j^2)>L_Creutz,j+D_KP,j`, which chooses a
  single `sigma_j` passing both the upstream Paper-15 reserve and the
  downstream marked-KP reserve;
- reduce the cofinal marked bridge to `AYM-CONF-MARK`: every cofinal battery
  proves `MARK-GEOM_j`, `MARK-LOSS_j`, and `MS-KP_j` with finite constants on
  the same whole-process tower;
- sharpen `AYM-CONF-WIN` to the map-level certificate
  `AYM-CONF-WIN-MAP`, specifying the maps
  `G_j -> D_CR,j -> B_15,j`, structural Paper-15 pass data, closure-loop
  compatibility, cofinality, and projective consistency;
- sharpen `AYM-CONF-LMOD` to `AYM-CONF-LMOD-EST`, with explicit bounds
  `underline kappa_j`, `overline E_j`, and `overline omega_j` satisfying the
  strict `delta_req,j<S_15,j/(2 ell_j^2)` margin;
- sharpen `AYM-CONF-MARK` to `AYM-CONF-MARK-UNIF`, one cofinal marked
  endpoint protocol with explicit geometry, local-loss, and marked-KP
  bounding sequences;
- compute the single-window margin
  `Gamma_j=alpha_j(S_15,j-2 delta_j ell_j^2)-L_Creutz,j-D_KP,j`; with the
  canonical midpoint choice of `sigma_j`, prove
  `G_j^Creutz=Gamma_j/2`;
- reduce `AYM-CONF-RATE` to the computable rate certificate
  `AYM-CONF-RATE-CALC(m_*)`:
  `inf_j[Gamma_j/(2 ell_j)-Delta_conf,j]>=2m_*>0`;
- strengthen the reserve target to `AYM-CONF-RES-NC`, giving explicit
  lower bounds
  `underline S_15,j=underline gamma_j underline M_j-overline epsilon_15,j>0`;
- sharpen the source estimates to `AYM-CONF-LMOD-SRC` and
  `AYM-CONF-MARK-SRC`, which prove the loop-modulus and marked-bridge
  workbench gates from actual heat-kernel/Wilson-comparison scalar record
  estimates;
- introduce the termwise lower margin
  `underline Gamma_j=underline alpha_j(underline S_15,j-2 overline delta_j ell_j^2)-overline L_j-overline D_j`;
- reduce the actual confinement rate to
  `AYM-CONF-GAMMA-LB(m_*)`:
  `inf_j[underline Gamma_j/(2 ell_j)-overline Delta_j]>=2m_*>0`;
- record the Paper-18 obstruction theorem: if the route fails despite
  `AYM-CONF-LAW` and `AYM-CONF-WP`, then window maps, reserve noncollapse,
  source loop-modulus, source marked bridge, termwise Gamma lower bound, or
  same-ledger compatibility must fail;
- sharpen those obstructions into the seven source certificates:
  `AYM-CONF-LAW-SRC`, `AYM-CONF-WIN-SRC`, `AYM-CONF-RES-SRC`,
  `AYM-CONF-LMOD-CALC`, `AYM-CONF-MARK-CALC`,
  `AYM-CONF-GAMMA-CALC(m_*)`, and `AYM-CONF-LEDGER-AUDIT`;
- import the law source from Paper 16 by proving
  `P16-LAW-IMPORT => AYM-CONF-LAW-SRC => AYM-CONF-LAW`, where
  `P16-LAW-IMPORT` consists of `HK-CYC-CLOSE`, Paper-18 loop-family
  admissibility, Paper-16 whole-process restrictions, and the no-hidden
  ontology clause;
- construct the cofinal window source explicitly by proving
  `AYM-CONF-WIN-SCHED => AYM-CONF-WIN-SRC => AYM-CONF-WIN-MAP`, where
  `AYM-CONF-WIN-SCHED` maps each Paper-17 cofinal probe battery `G_j` to a
  nested finite Creutz window `D_CR,j`, a finite Paper-15 battery `B_15,j`,
  scalar inclusion maps `iota_j`, and finite probe-support maps `pi_j`;
- reduce the reserve source to the explicit cofinal calculation
  `AYM-CONF-RES-CALC => AYM-CONF-RES-SRC => AYM-CONF-RES-NC`, where
  `underline M_j` is the Paper-16 surface reserve lower bound minus the
  battery, regulator, volume, and loop-shape loss upper bounds, and the hard
  reserve inequality is
  `underline gamma_j underline M_j-overline epsilon_15,j>0`;
- discharge the reserve calculation symbolically or numerically by proving
  `AYM-CONF-RES-SYM => AYM-CONF-RES-CALC`, where the verifier expands
  `underline M_SUB,j` into the Paper-15 leading-character term, decoration
  loss, and prior transport loss, or by proving the finite-prefix/uniform-tail
  criterion `AYM-CONF-RES-TAIL => AYM-CONF-RES-CALC`;
- reduce the actual cofinal reserve source to
  `AYM-CONF-RES-ACT-TAIL => AYM-CONF-RES-TAIL`, where the actual tail must
  export Paper-16 `HK-CREUTZ-CLOSE_j`, a uniform transported reserve
  `M_R>0`, a normalization lower bound `gamma_R>0`, an alignment-loss upper
  bound `epsilon_R`, and the hard positive reserve
  `gamma_R M_R-epsilon_R>=s_R>0`;
- sharpen the actual reserve-tail attempt to the real-constant criterion
  `AYM-CONF-RES-RC-TAIL => AYM-CONF-RES-ACT-TAIL`, with
  `M_R=(u_R^-)^{N_R}(1-(u_R^+)^{Q_R})-Delta_R-T_R
  -L_bat,R-L_reg,R-L_vol,R-L_shape,R`; this proves the tail only on a
  uniformly local/bounded-geometry branch, while the raw growing-sheet branch
  `N_0,j->infinity` with `u_{-,j}<=u_max<1` falsifies any positive absolute
  cofinal `M_R`;
- discharge the loop-modulus calculation symbolically or numerically by
  proving `AYM-CONF-LMOD-SYM => AYM-CONF-LMOD-CALC`, where the verifier
  exports the positive Creutz-slot denominator `underline kappa_j`, the
  transported loop-modulus bound `overline omega_j`, the readout bound
  `overline E_j`, and the strict comparison
  `max{overline E_j/ell_j^2, 4 overline omega_j/(underline kappa_j ell_j^2)}
  < underline S_15,j/(2 ell_j^2)`, or by proving the finite-prefix/uniform-tail
  criterion `AYM-CONF-LMOD-TAIL => AYM-CONF-LMOD-CALC`;
- reduce the actual loop-modulus source to
  `AYM-CONF-LMOD-ACT-SYM => AYM-CONF-LMOD-SYM`, where the actual continuum
  trajectory must export finite-window Creutz-slot positivity, finite-stage
  slot transport, loop-continuity errors, readout errors, and the same strict
  comparison to `underline S_15,j`; the stronger tail route
  `AYM-CONF-LMOD-ACT-TAIL => AYM-CONF-LMOD-TAIL` additionally requires a
  uniform normalized denominator `kappa_L>0` and normalized tail errors
  `max{e_L,w_L}<s_L/2`;
- decide the actual loop-modulus tail by the real-constant criterion
  `AYM-CONF-LMOD-RC-TAIL => AYM-CONF-LMOD-ACT-TAIL`, requiring a uniform
  positive raw or normalized slot denominator `kappa_L>0`, normalized reserve
  `S_15,j/ell_j^2>=s_L`, finite-stage slot transport, normalized readout and
  loop-modulus errors, and `max{e_L,w_L}<s_L/2`; raw growing slots with
  `W(L_j)->0`, for example area-decaying loops with
  `W(L_j)<=C exp[-sigma A_j+K P_j+K_0]->0`, falsify the absolute tail route
  and force finite-window `AYM-CONF-LMOD-ACT-SYM` or denominator-normalized
  records;
- discharge the marked-bridge calculation symbolically or numerically by
  proving `AYM-CONF-MARK-SYM => AYM-CONF-MARK-CALC`, where the verifier
  exports the finite endpoint closure rule, `alpha_j>=alpha_*>0`,
  `N_cl,j<=N_*<infinity`, the local marked-loss bound
  `epsilon_area,j<=overline epsilon_j`, the endpoint-enlarged marked KP
  bounds `h_j^S<=overline h_j`, `lambda_mark,j^S<=overline lambda_j`,
  `D_KP,j<=overline D_j`, and the uniform character-tail bound
  `eta_ch,j<=eta_*<1`, or by proving the finite-prefix/uniform-tail criterion
  `AYM-CONF-MARK-TAIL => AYM-CONF-MARK-CALC`;
- reduce the actual endpoint-enlarged marked KP source to
  `AYM-CONF-MARK-ACT-SYM => AYM-CONF-MARK-SYM`, where the actual trajectory
  must build same-ledger endpoint-enlarged finite batteries `B_j^S`, prove
  Paper-14 `FBE_j^S`, prove positive Paper-15 `nCPSC_j^S`, debit a finite
  endpoint-marking ledger, and keep `eta_ch,j<=eta_*<1`; the stronger tail
  route is now sharpened by
  `AYM-CONF-MARK-RC-TAIL => AYM-CONF-MARK-ACT-TAIL` and then
  `AYM-CONF-MARK-ACT-TAIL => AYM-CONF-MARK-TAIL`, requiring one cofinal
  endpoint closure/loss convention, finite endpoint-enlarged KP thresholds
  on the tail, and a uniform `eta_ch,j<=eta_M<1`; pointwise
  `eta_ch,j<1` does not prove the tail if `sup_j eta_ch,j=1`;
- execute the first three source-constant campaign steps explicitly:
  `AYM-CONF-TOWER-FRZ` freezes one whole-process tower and debit ledger,
  `AYM-CONF-LAWWIN-AUDIT` proves
  `AYM-CONF-LAW-SRC + AYM-CONF-WIN-SRC` on that tower, and
  `AYM-CONF-RES-ATTACK` decides whether the reserve source has
  finite-window success, absolute-tail success, normalized-tail survival
  into the Gamma ledger, or a genuine reserve-source obstruction;
- execute the loop-modulus constant attack:
  `AYM-CONF-LMOD-CONST-ATTACK` computes `K_j^slot`,
  `underline kappa_j`, `overline E_j`, `overline omega_j`,
  `delta_req,j`, and `delta_max,j=underline S_15,j/(2 ell_j^2)`, then
  decides finite-window LMOD success, uniform-tail LMOD success, normalized
  Gamma survival through positive `q_j`, or a genuine loop-modulus
  obstruction;
- execute the marked-bridge constant attack:
  `AYM-CONF-MARK-CONST-ATTACK` builds endpoint-enlarged batteries `B_j^S`,
  verifies `FBE_j^S` and positive `nCPSC_j^S`, computes
  `overline epsilon_j`, `overline h_j`, `overline lambda_j`,
  `overline D_j`, `eta_ch,j`, and
  `b_j^MARK=(overline L_j^MARK+overline D_j)/(2 ell_j)`, then decides
  finite-window MARK success, uniform-tail MARK success with
  `eta_ch,j<=eta_M<1`, normalized Gamma survival through bounded
  `b_j^MARK`, or a genuine marked-bridge obstruction;
- execute the Gamma-rate constant attack:
  `AYM-CONF-GAMMA-CONST-ATTACK(m_*)` assembles
  `Q_j=underline S_15,j-2 overline delta_j ell_j^2`,
  `overline L_j=overline epsilon_j+overline h_j+overline lambda_j`,
  `underline Gamma_j=underline alpha_j Q_j-overline L_j-overline D_j`,
  `r_j=underline Gamma_j/(2 ell_j)-overline Delta_j`,
  and the normalized tail constants `q_G`, `b_G`, `Delta_G`; it then
  decides finite-window Gamma success, compact-tail Gamma success,
  smaller-rate survival, or a genuine Gamma-rate obstruction;
- assemble the final Gamma-rate calculation by proving
  `AYM-CONF-GAMMA-SYM(m_*) => AYM-CONF-GAMMA-CALC(m_*)`, where
  `overline L_j=overline epsilon_j+overline h_j+overline lambda_j`,
  `underline Gamma_j=underline alpha_j(underline S_15,j
  -2 overline delta_j ell_j^2)-overline L_j-overline D_j`, and the hard
  inequality is
  `inf_j[underline Gamma_j/(2 ell_j)-overline Delta_j]>=2m_*>0`, or by
  proving the finite-prefix/uniform-tail criterion
  `AYM-CONF-GAMMA-TAIL(m_*) => AYM-CONF-GAMMA-CALC(m_*)`;
- reduce the actual physical Gamma-rate source to
  `AYM-CONF-GAMMA-ACT-SYM(m_*) => AYM-CONF-GAMMA-SYM(m_*)`, where the actual
  trajectory must assemble same-ledger reserve, loop-modulus, marked-bridge,
  and Paper-17 debit bounds and prove
  `r_j=underline Gamma_j/(2 ell_j)-overline Delta_j>=2m_*>0`; the stronger
  tail route is now sharpened by
  `AYM-CONF-GAMMA-RC-TAIL(m_*) => AYM-CONF-GAMMA-ACT-TAIL(m_*)` and then
  `AYM-CONF-GAMMA-ACT-TAIL(m_*) => AYM-CONF-GAMMA-TAIL(m_*)`, where
  `q_G` is the cofinal tail infimum of
  `(underline S_15,j-2 overline delta_j ell_j^2)/ell_j`, `b_G` is the
  cofinal tail supremum of `(overline L_j+overline D_j)/(2 ell_j)`,
  `Delta_G` is the cofinal tail supremum of `overline Delta_j`, and the
  compact tail succeeds exactly when
  `alpha_G q_G/2-b_G-Delta_G>=2m_*>0`;
- prove the source-closure implication
  `AYM-CONF-LAW-SRC + AYM-CONF-WIN-SRC + AYM-CONF-RES-SRC
  + AYM-CONF-LMOD-CALC + AYM-CONF-MARK-CALC
  + AYM-CONF-GAMMA-CALC(m_*) + AYM-CONF-LEDGER-AUDIT
  => AYM-CONF-CLOSE(m_*)`;
- discharge the ledger-audit gate by importing `HK-WP-CLOSE`, `MG-WP`, and
  `CONF-WP` onto one common refinement and adding the explicit no-double-debit
  register `CONF-DEBIT-REG`, giving
  `CONF-IMPORT-WP => AYM-CONF-LEDGER-AUDIT => AYM-CONF-WP`;
- prove
  `AYM-CONF-CLOSE(m_*) => COF-P15-CREUTZ(m_*) => MGAP(m_*)`;
- record the no-smuggling principle: strong-coupling area law, flux-tube
  pictures, gauge-fixed sheets, or partial kernels are not confinement
  inputs unless they export one of the scalar record certificates above;
- convert the confinement certificate into the Paper-17 dynamical inputs:
  `G_j-2PT-KP` for every cofinal probe battery and `MG-UNIF(m_*)`;
- track the same cutoff, volume, smearing, block, battery, regulator, and
  projective losses used by Paper 17;
- enforce `CONF-WP`, the whole-process confinement ledger preventing
  Markovian partial-kernel composition and preventing charged boundary
  instruments from being mistaken for scalar Gamma records;
- state the precise completion gate for a 4D pure quantum gauge theory:
  `CYM_WL + MG-OS-CLOSE + cofinal MG-OBS + G_j-2PT-KP + MG-UNIF + MG-WP`;
- express confinement in ISP terms: colored charged records are typed
  instruments and boundary probes, not isolated scalar Gamma records.

Key reduction target:

```text
CONF-REC
+ CONF-WP
+ [CR-MTD + CR-LMOD => CR-DOM^cof]
+ [CH-BDY-PROT => CH-BDY]
+ CONF-AL(sigma) or CONF-CR(sigma)
+ [MARK-GEOM_j + MARK-LOSS_j => AL2MARK_j(sigma)]
+ AL2MARK_j(sigma) => CONF-MARK_j(sigma) for every cofinal battery
+ MS-KP_j for every cofinal battery
+ G_j-CONF-PASS for every cofinal battery
+ CONF-COFINAL-PASS(m_*)
=> G_j-2PT-KP for all j
+ MG-UNIF(m_*)
=> Paper-17 MGAP(m_*).
```

First-battery checkpoint:

```text
CONF-REC + CONF-WP
+ direct CONF-AL(sigma)
+ [G_box block-face hulls => MARK-GEOM_box]
+ [same-ledger local loss bounds => MARK-LOSS_box]
+ [MARK-GEOM_box + MARK-LOSS_box => AL2MARK_box(sigma)]
+ [Paper-14 FBE_box + Paper-15 nCPSC_box + endpoint marking
   => BOX-MSKP-IMPORT => MS-KP_box]
+ BOX-RESERVE-PASS(clean)
=> BOX-CONF-PASS
=> BOX-2PT-KP
```

Creutz fallback checkpoint:

```text
CONF-REC + CONF-WP
+ [P15-CREUTZ-PASS_box, including
   S_15,box >= (sigma+2 delta_box)s_0^2
   => CONF-CR_box(sigma)]
+ [CR-LMOD-QUANT_box => CR-LMOD_box]
+ [G_box block-face hulls => MARK-GEOM_box]
+ [same-ledger local loss bounds => MARK-LOSS_box]
+ [MARK-GEOM_box + MARK-LOSS_box => AL2MARK_box(sigma)]
+ [Paper-14 FBE_box + Paper-15 nCPSC_box + endpoint marking
   => BOX-MSKP-IMPORT => MS-KP_box]
+ [alpha_box(S_15,box - 2 delta_box s_0^2)
   > L_Creutz,box + D_KP,box]
+ BOX-RESERVE-PASS(Creutz)
=> BOX-CONF-PASS
=> BOX-2PT-KP
```

Branch worksheet and explicit clustering checkpoint:

```text
A_box^branch = available clean/Creutz branches
R_best,box = max_{beta in A_box^branch} R_beta,box
R_best,box > D_KP,box
=> BOX-RESERVE-PASS(beta_best)
=> BOX-CONF-PASS
```

and with Paper 17 `BOX-MASS` for an admissible selected rate:

```text
R_beta,box > D_KP,box
+ BOX-MASS
=> MG-EXP-CLOSE(m_phys,box) on G_box.
```

Paper-15 Creutz specialization:

```text
P15-CREUTZ-PASS_box
+ BOX-MSKP-IMPORT
+ MARK-GEOM_box
+ MARK-LOSS_box
+ R_Creutz,box > D_KP,box
+ [G_box^Creutz > s_0 Delta_tot,box => BOX-MASS]
=> MG-EXP-CLOSE(m_phys,box) on G_box.
```

Cofinal checkpoint:

```text
G_j-CONF-PASS for every j
+ selected-rate reserve
=> G_j-2PT-KP for every j
+ MG-UNIF(m_*).
```

Cofinal Paper-15 Creutz checkpoint:

```text
P15-CREUTZ-PASS_j for every cofinal G_j
+ MARK-GEOM_j + MARK-LOSS_j + MS-KP_j
+ inf_j [G_j^Creutz/ell_j - Delta_conf,j] >= 2m_* > 0
=> COF-P15-CREUTZ(m_*)
=> CONF-COFINAL-PASS(m_*)
=> MGAP(m_*).
```

Actual `4D SU(N)` confinement checkpoint:

```text
CYM_WL on one actual whole-process trajectory
+ cofinal Paper-15 Creutz windows
+ S_15,j>0 with quantitative CR-LMOD-QUANT_j
+ alpha_j(S_15,j - 2 delta_j ell_j^2)
   > L_Creutz,j + D_KP,j
+ MARK-GEOM_j + MARK-LOSS_j + MS-KP_j on the same tower
+ canonical G_j^Creutz = Gamma_j/2
+ inf_j [Gamma_j/(2 ell_j) - Delta_conf,j] >= 2m_* > 0
+ termwise lower bound:
  underline Gamma_j
  = underline alpha_j(underline S_15,j-2 overline delta_j ell_j^2)
    - overline L_j - overline D_j
+ inf_j [underline Gamma_j/(2 ell_j) - overline Delta_j] >= 2m_* > 0
=> AYM-CONF-CLOSE(m_*)
=> COF-P15-CREUTZ(m_*)
=> MGAP(m_*).
```

Workbench split:

```text
AYM-CONF-LAW  -> CYM_WL from HK-CYC-CLOSE
AYM-CONF-WIN  -> cofinal G_j to D_CR,j, Paper-15 battery alignment,
                 and structural Paper-15 pass data
                 via AYM-CONF-WIN-MAP
AYM-CONF-RES  -> P15-RES-CAL_j for all j:
                 HK-CREUTZ-CLOSE_j gives M_15,j^bd>0,
                 epsilon_15_to_j<gamma_15,j M_15,j^bd
                 gives S_15,j>0
                 strengthened by AYM-CONF-RES-NC
AYM-CONF-LMOD -> AYM-CONF-LMOD-EST quantitative denominator/error/modulus
                 sourced by AYM-CONF-LMOD-SRC, with actual finite-window
                 source AYM-CONF-LMOD-ACT-SYM and stronger tail source
                 AYM-CONF-LMOD-ACT-TAIL only after LMOD-RC-TAIL or
                 denominator-normalized records
AYM-CONF-SWIN -> AYM-CONF-SWIN-CALC with Gamma_j>0
AYM-CONF-MARK -> AYM-CONF-MARK-UNIF for all cofinal j
                 sourced by AYM-CONF-MARK-SRC, with actual finite-window
                 source AYM-CONF-MARK-ACT-SYM and stronger tail source
                 AYM-CONF-MARK-RC-TAIL => AYM-CONF-MARK-ACT-TAIL
                 when eta_ch,j<=eta_M<1 uniformly
AYM-CONF-RATE -> AYM-CONF-RATE-CALC:
                 inf_j[Gamma_j/(2 ell_j)-Delta_conf,j]>=2m_*>0
                 or termwise AYM-CONF-GAMMA-LB:
                 inf_j[underline Gamma_j/(2 ell_j)-overline Delta_j]>=2m_*>0
                 with actual finite-window source AYM-CONF-GAMMA-ACT-SYM
                 and stronger tail source
                 AYM-CONF-GAMMA-RC-TAIL => AYM-CONF-GAMMA-ACT-TAIL
                 after q_G,b_G,Delta_G pass the final margin test
AYM-CONF-WP   -> one whole-process tower and one debit ledger.
```

Definition target:

```text
4D pure quantum gauge theory in ISP
:= a whole-process Wilson-loop record law satisfying
   CYM_WL + MG-OS-CLOSE + cofinal MG-OBS + MG-WP,
   with confinement/mass-gap completion gates when the dynamical estimates
   G_j-2PT-KP and MG-UNIF hold.
```

Pass condition:

- a positive string tension or equivalent confinement theorem on the declared
  continuum target, plus `CONF-REC`, `CONF-WP`, `AL2MARK_j`,
  `CONF-MARK_j`, `MS-KP_j`, `G_j-CONF-PASS`, and
  `CONF-COFINAL-PASS(m_*)`, yielding a rigorous implication to
  `G_j-2PT-KP` and `MG-UNIF(m_*)`.

Fail condition:

- only strong-coupling finite-regulator area laws or perimeter laws are
  controlled;
- confinement estimates hold only on fixed finite batteries and do not give a
  cofinal marked two-point KP bound;
- the debited rate reserve vanishes in the cofinal or continuum limit.

## V3 Paper 19: Actual Source Constants For 4D `SU(N)` Confinement

Suggested title:

`Actual Source Constants For The ISP Confinement Closure`

Draft:

`relativistic-isp-v3-paper19-actual-source-constants-confinement.md`

Main question:

> Do the actual continuum `4D SU(N)` Wilson-loop records supply the source
> constants needed by Paper 18's minimal-debit confinement closure?

Main job:

- start from Paper 18's final source-gate checklist, not from a new
  confinement architecture;
- prove or falsify `AYM-CONF-ACT-CRES-P16(c_R)`: Paper 16/Paper 15 must
  export a same-ledger raw surface reserve, or an already-debited reserve
  with no Paper-18 double counting;
- prove or falsify `AYM-CONF-ACT-KQ-RATE(W_R)`: the Paper-16
  loop-continuity selector must drive loop/readout error below the moving
  Creutz-denominator scale;
- test the scalar reserve-loop threshold
  `c_R >= C_quot^crit(s_R,W_R)`, equivalently
  `S_j^RLD>0` cofinally after the minimal legal loop-modulus debit;
- only after the reserve-loop gate passes, prove or falsify
  `AYM-CONF-ACT-PI-SRC-IMPORT(s_R,m_*)` and
  `AYM-CONF-ACT-PI-THRESH(s_P,m_*)`;
- audit `AYM-CONF-ACT-LEDGER-SRC`: all constants must be restrictions of one
  frozen whole-process law with one disjoint debit register;
- audit `AYM-CONF-ACT-COF-SRC(s_R,s_P,m_*)`: the passing windows must form a
  cofinal scheduled family with the same positive margins.

Pass condition:

- the actual source gates imply Paper 18's final conditional theorem:

  ```text
  P16-LAW-IMPORT
  + AYM-CONF-WIN-SCHED
  + AYM-CONF-ACT-CRES-P16(c_R)
  + AYM-CONF-ACT-KQ-RATE(W_R)
  + c_R >= C_quot^crit(s_R,W_R)
  + AYM-CONF-ACT-PI-SRC-IMPORT(s_R,m_*)
  + AYM-CONF-ACT-PI-THRESH(s_P,m_*)
  + AYM-CONF-ACT-LEDGER-SRC
  + AYM-CONF-ACT-COF-SRC(s_R,s_P,m_*)
  => AYM-CONF-CLOSE(m_*)
  => MGAP(m_*).
  ```

Fail condition:

- the reserve-loop threshold fails, the pressure threshold fails, the
  same-ledger audit fails, or finite-window successes cannot be scheduled
  cofinally. In that case Paper 19 must name the obstruction rather than
  claiming confinement.

Why this matters:

Paper 18 shows that the route is algebraically and ontologically clean. Paper
19 is the first place where the program must either produce actual
nonperturbative `4D SU(N)` source constants or admit that the confinement
closure remains conditional.

Current status:

- Draft started in
  `physics/relativistic-isp-v3-paper19-actual-source-constants-confinement.md`.
- The first pass imports the Paper-18 final source checklist, defines the
  structural frozen source tower `P19-TOWER`, and proves the source-closure
  theorem:

  ```text
  P19-TOWER
  + P16-LAW-IMPORT
  + AYM-CONF-WIN-SCHED
  + [P19-CRES-RAW(c_R) or P19-CRES-DEB(c_R)]
  + P19-KQ-SRC(W_R)
  + P19-RLD-THRESH(c_R,W_R,s_R)
  + P19-PI-SRC(s_R,m_*)
  + P19-PI-THRESH(s_P,m_*)
  + P19-COF(s_R,s_P,m_*)
  => AYM-CONF-CLOSE(m_*)
  => MGAP(m_*).
  ```

  After the 2026-05-22 boundary audit, `P19-TOWER` is explicitly split into
  finite restrictions, readout/window compatibility, debit bookkeeping, and
  scale declaration. It is not an area-law assumption and does not include
  `R_H^opt<R_H^crit`, `L_AFM^sharp<Sig_AFM`, a positive string tension, or a
  continuum Yang-Mills existence theorem.

- The first open bottleneck is the scalar reserve-loop margin

  ```text
  s_R^max
  =
  gamma_R(c_R-L_R)-e_R-2 max{E_R,4W_R}
  > 0.
  ```

  This requires proving or falsifying the reserve lower bound `c_R` and the
  quotient loop-modulus constant `W_R` on one actual whole-process tower.

- The Step-1 decision layer is now explicit in Paper 19. The guessed
  constants have been replaced by sharp tail envelopes:

  ```text
  c_b^tail = liminf_j R_b,j,
  W^tail = limsup_j inf_alpha Xi_j(alpha)/d_j(alpha),
  s_R,route^tail
  =
  max_b [gamma_R(c_b^tail-L_R,b)-e_R-2 max{E_R,4W^tail}].
  ```

  If `s_R,route^tail>0`, the reserve-loop gate is proved. If
  `s_R,route^tail<=0` using sharp same-ledger envelopes, the Paper-18
  minimal-debit route is falsified for the declared tower and window
  schedule. The current Papers 15--16 do not yet supply those sharp tail
  envelopes, so Paper 19 has fully reduced Step 1 but has not yet proved or
  falsified actual `4D SU(N)` confinement.

- Step 1a now isolates the already-debited reserve envelope:

  ```text
  c_deb^tail = liminf_j M_15,j^bd
             = liminf_j (M_SUB,j^bd-L_bat,j-L_reg,j-L_vol,j-L_shape,j).
  ```

  It proves the exact branch verdict:

  ```text
  c_deb^tail>0  => debited reserve branch passes,
  c_deb^tail<=0 => debited reserve branch cannot supply c_R>0.
  ```

  Component tests are now explicit:

  ```text
  liminf M_SUB,j^bd > limsup(L_bat,j+L_reg,j+L_vol,j+L_shape,j)
  => c_deb^tail>0,

  limsup M_SUB,j^bd <= liminf(L_bat,j+L_reg,j+L_vol,j+L_shape,j)
  => c_deb^tail<=0.
  ```

  The direct Paper-15 witness gives the analogous test using
  `u_-^{N_0}(1-u_+^{Q_sigma})` against `Delta_dec^bd+T_loss^bd`. Current
  source papers do not yet decide these envelope inequalities.

- The direct Paper-15 witness has now been pushed one level deeper. Paper 19
  rewrites the signal as

  ```text
  A_j = exp(-Theta_j)(1-exp(-Phi_j)),
  Theta_j = N_0,j (-log u_-,j),
  Phi_j = Q_sigma,j (-log u_+,j).
  ```

  The explicit positive source route is:

  ```text
  limsup Theta_j <= Theta_* < infinity,
  liminf Phi_j >= Phi_* > 0,
  limsup Delta_dec,j^bd <= D_*,
  limsup T_loss,j^bd <= T_*,
  exp(-Theta_*)(1-exp(-Phi_*)) > D_*+T_*
  => c_15^tail > 0.
  ```

  The corresponding falsification route compares an upper signal ceiling
  `exp(-Theta_0)(1-exp(-Phi^*))` against a lower loss floor. Thus the next
  actual mathematical work is no longer algebraic: estimate `Theta_j`,
  `Phi_j`, decoration losses, and transport losses on the actual continuum
  tower.

- The leading-sheet exponent `Theta_j` has now been separated. Paper 19
  proves:

  ```text
  limsup N_0,j(-log u_-,j) <= Theta_* < infinity
  <=> liminf u_-,j^{N_0,j} >= exp(-Theta_*) > 0.
  ```

  Sufficient routes:

  ```text
  fixed finite Creutz window:
    N_0,j <= N_* and u_-,j >= u_*^- > 0;

  heat-kernel scaling:
    limsup N_0,j t_j C_2(rho_j)/2 < infinity
    and limsup N_0,j[-log(1-eta_j)] < infinity.
  ```

  Obstruction:

  ```text
  N_0,j -> infinity and u_-,j <= u^+ < 1
  => Theta_j -> infinity.
  ```

  Therefore fixed batteries bound `Theta_j`, but a growing-window area-law
  route must prove `-log u_-,j=O(1/N_0,j)`.

- The first-excess exponent `Phi_j` has now been separated and compared
  against `Theta_j`. Paper 19 proves:

  ```text
  liminf Q_sigma,j(-log u_+,j) >= Phi_* > 0
  <=> liminf (1-u_+,j^{Q_sigma,j}) >= 1-exp(-Phi_*) > 0.
  ```

  Fixed finite Creutz windows pass this gate if
  `Q_sigma,j>=Q_*>0` and `u_+,j<=u^+<1`. For growing-window schedules, the
  compatibility theorem says that if `Theta_j` is bounded and the upper/lower
  coefficient exponents are comparable, then:

  ```text
  Q_sigma,j/N_0,j -> 0
  => Phi_j -> 0.
  ```

  Thus the standard comparable-window direct witness needs
  `liminf Q_sigma,j/N_0,j>0` in addition to the leading-coefficient scaling.

- The Creutz window geometry has now been computed for the standard
  rectangular battery. For block areas `N_{R,T}=RT`,

  ```text
  Q_sigma = sigma^2,
  N_0 = 2RT - sigma(R+T),
  Q_sigma/N_0 = sigma^2/[2RT - sigma(R+T)].
  ```

  Consequence: fixed or sub-macroscopic `sigma` on growing rectangles makes
  `Q_sigma/N_0 -> 0`, so the direct Paper-15 witness cannot keep `Phi_j`
  positive under bounded `Theta_j` and comparable coefficient exponents.
  Thick/co-scaling windows repair the geometry gate. For square windows
  `R=T=L`, `sigma=alpha L`, one gets

  ```text
  Q_sigma/N_0 = alpha^2/[2(1-alpha)] > 0.
  ```

  This only removes the geometric obstruction; Paper 19 still needs the
  coefficient, decoration-loss, transport-loss, and same-ledger debit
  estimates on the same declared window schedule.

- Paper 19 has now promoted thick/co-scaling windows into the main
  growing-window direct-witness branch. The declared branch uses an area
  scale `S_j=R_jT_j` with

  ```text
  Q_sigma,j/S_j >= q_- > 0,
  N_0,j/S_j <= n_+ < infinity.
  ```

  The reciprocal-area coefficient gate is:

  ```text
  limsup S_j [t_j C_2(rho_j)/2 - log(1-eta_j)] <= A_*,
  liminf S_j [t_j C_2(rho_j)/2 - log(1+zeta_j)] >= B_* > 0.
  ```

  Under this gate, Paper 19 proves:

  ```text
  Theta_* = n_+ A_*,
  Phi_* = q_- B_*.
  ```

  Hence the thick-window direct witness passes if the loss side satisfies:

  ```text
  exp(-n_+ A_*)[1-exp(-q_- B_*)]
  > exp(c_Delta^* eta_*/(1-eta_*))-1 + T_*.
  ```

  It also proves the matching obstruction: under comparable coefficient
  exponents, if the exponent scale is below reciprocal area then `Phi_j`
  collapses, while if it is above reciprocal area then `Theta_j` diverges.
  So the viable cofinal direct-witness regime is now sharply identified as
  `-log u_{\pm,j} ~ 1/S_j`.

- The reciprocal-area coefficient source has now been reduced to a clean
  heat-kernel time schedule plus two error-width budgets. Paper 19 defines:

  ```text
  Acal_j = S_j t_j C_2(rho_j)/2,
  Eminus_j = S_j[-log(1-eta_j)],
  Eplus_j = S_j log(1+zeta_j).
  ```

  If

  ```text
  liminf Acal_j >= A^-,
  limsup Acal_j <= A^+,
  limsup Eminus_j <= E^-,
  limsup Eplus_j <= E^+,
  A^- > E^+,
  ```

  then the thick coefficient gate holds with

  ```text
  A_* = A^+ + E^-,
  B_* = A^- - E^+ > 0.
  ```

  The clean route is `t_j=beta_j/S_j`; for fixed `rho`, this gives
  `A^- = beta_- C_2(rho)/2` and `A^+ = beta_+ C_2(rho)/2`. The remaining
  actual-source problem is to prove, on the Paper-16 whole-process tower,
  that the character coefficient errors obey the reciprocal-area bounds and
  that `beta_- C_2(rho)/2` dominates the upper error budget.

- Paper 19 has now compared the clean `t_j=beta_j/S_j` route with the
  Paper-16 heat-kernel asymptotically-free trajectory. Since Paper 16 uses

  ```text
  t_i = g_i^2 + O(g_i^4),
  g_i^{-2}
    = 2 beta_0 log(1/(a_i Lambda))
      + (beta_1/beta_0) log log(1/(a_i Lambda))
      + O(1),
  ```

  the clean reciprocal-area route is compatible with Paper 16 exactly when

  ```text
  S_j = R_j T_j ~ g_i^{-2}.
  ```

  For square thick windows this means

  ```text
  L_j^2 ~ g_i^{-2},
  L_j ~ g_i^{-1} ~ sqrt(log(1/a_i)).
  ```

  If `S_j << g_i^{-2}`, the clean first-excess source collapses. If
  `S_j >> g_i^{-2}`, the clean leading-sheet source diverges. Thus the viable
  direct-witness branch is now an AF-matched logarithmic cofinal window
  schedule, and the next source problem is the coefficient-error budget on
  that schedule.

- Paper 19 has now finished the AF-matched coefficient-error reduction. On
  the AF-matched branch, Paper 14's additive coefficient error `delta_j`
  enters through

  ```text
  r_j = delta_j exp(a_j).
  ```

  Since `S_j ~ g_i^{-2}`, the required error scale is

  ```text
  r_j = O(g_i^2).
  ```

  More precisely, if `limsup g_i^{-2} r_j <= R_H` and
  `r_j <= r_* < 1` cofinally, then the coefficient-error budgets are

  ```text
  E^+ = s_+ R_H,
  E^- = s_+ R_H/(1-r_*).
  ```

  The coefficient source passes when

  ```text
  (1-chi) s_- C_2(rho)/2 > s_+ R_H.
  ```

- The coefficient-error estimate has now been attacked against the Paper-14
  rate class. Paper 14 supplies a polynomial coefficient-error rate
  `delta_j <= C_CE n_j^{-1-p_CE}`. Paper 19 proves that this implies

  ```text
  r_j = delta_j exp(a_j) = O(g_i^2)
  ```

  provided the standard chain is calibrated by

  ```text
  log(1/(a_i Lambda)) <= C_L n_i^{1+p_CE}.
  ```

  Equivalently, ordinary exponential-in-index lattice refinement
  `a_i Lambda ~ exp(-c n_i^kappa)` works when `kappa <= 1+p_CE`. Without
  such calibration the Paper-14 rate class alone is too weak to prove the
  AF-scaled estimate, although it does not falsify the actual coefficient
  error. The small-constant condition
  `(1-chi)s_-C_2(rho)/2 > s_+R_H` is resolved by the sharp `R_H^opt`
  test below.

- Paper 19 has now resolved the coefficient-error constant itself as a sharp
  limsup on the declared whole-process tower:

  ```text
  R_H^opt = limsup_j g_i^{-2} delta_j exp(a_j).
  ```

  The Section-8J coefficient route passes exactly when

  ```text
  R_H^opt < R_H^crit,
  R_H^crit = (1-chi)s_- C_2(rho)/(2s_+).
  ```

  Combining Paper 14's coefficient-error rate with Paper 16's AF running
  gives the source bound

  ```text
  R_H^opt <= 2 beta_0 K_CE K_L,
  K_CE = limsup n_j^{1+p_CE} delta_j,
  K_L = limsup log(1/(a_i Lambda))/n_j^{1+p_CE}.
  ```

  Therefore the coefficient-error source is discharged if
  `2 beta_0 K_CE K_L < R_H^crit`. The current source papers do not yet
  supply this strict same-tower product bound, and they do not provide lower
  bounds falsifying it.

- Paper 19 has now pushed the `R_H` problem beyond the coarse chain-index
  route. It introduces the AF-normalized coefficient-defect certificate

  ```text
  limsup_j delta_j/g_i^2 <= K_AF,
  ```

  which immediately gives `R_H^opt <= K_AF`. It then decomposes the
  coefficient defect into six same-ledger source errors:

  ```text
  delta_j <= delta_HK,j + delta_proj,j + delta_chart,j
           + delta_ct,j + delta_vol,j + delta_tail,j.
  ```

  The preferred source target is now:

  ```text
  K_HK+K_proj+K_chart+K_ct+K_vol+K_tail < R_H^crit,
  ```

  where each `K_*` is the AF-normalized limsup of the corresponding source
  defect. Paper 19 also records the threshold optimization:

  ```text
  s_-/s_+ > 2K_AF^src/[(1-chi)C_2(rho)].
  ```

  Paper 19 has now made that optimization explicit. A tight AF-area schedule
  means

  ```text
  s(1-epsilon_A) <= S_j/H_j <= s(1+epsilon_A),
  ```

  so the coefficient threshold becomes

  ```text
  R_H^crit(epsilon_A,chi,rho)
    = [(1-chi)(1-epsilon_A)/(1+epsilon_A)] C_2(rho)/2.
  ```

  Scheme slack is minimized by passing to a tail where
  `t_i/g_i^2 in [1-chi,1+chi]`. The representation selector is restricted to
  `R_adm(epsilon_A,chi)`, the channels whose tail, decoration, battery, and
  first-excess ledgers remain controlled. The optimized pass test is:

  ```text
  exists rho in R_adm(epsilon_A,chi):
    K_AF^src(rho) < R_H^crit(epsilon_A,chi,rho).
  ```

  If no controlled channel satisfies this even as `epsilon_A,chi -> 0`, then
  the Section-8J coefficient route fails; increasing `C_2(rho)` outside the
  controlled ledger is not an allowed shortcut.

- Paper 19 has now frozen the first selector candidate `SEL_0`. It uses the
  lowest nontrivial controlled channel `rho_0`:

  ```text
  rho_0 = fundamental or paired fundamental controlled record,
  L_j = floor(sqrt(s H_j)),
  sigma_j = floor(alpha L_j),
  S_j = L_j^2,
  S_j/H_j -> s.
  ```

  For any small `epsilon_A` and `chi`, the first-selector threshold is

  ```text
  R_0^crit
    = [(1-chi)(1-epsilon_A)/(1+epsilon_A)] C_2(rho_0)/2.
  ```

  The six-source ledger is now explicit:

  ```text
  K_0^src =
    K_HK^(0)+K_proj^(0)+K_chart^(0)
    +K_ct^(0)+K_vol^(0)+K_tail^(0).
  ```

  The first selector closes the coefficient source exactly if

  ```text
  K_0^src < R_0^crit.
  ```

  If `rho_0` fails tail, decoration, battery, or first-excess admissibility,
  `SEL_0` fails honestly. If `K_0^src >= R_0^crit`, only the first selector
  fails; another admissible channel may still be tested. The next concrete
  source attack is therefore `K_HK^(0)`, the heat-kernel reference defect on
  this frozen candidate.

- Paper 19 has now attacked `K_HK^(0)` in the correct order:
  decomposition first, branch choice second. For the fixed Paper-16
  heat-kernel time,

  ```text
  K_HK^(0)
    = limsup |u_0^act - exp(-t_i C_2(rho_0)/2)| / g_i^2.
  ```

  The heat-kernel reference defect is first split into four same-ledger
  debits:

  ```text
  K_HK^(0)
    <= K_time^(0)+K_block^(0)+K_cross^(0)+K_extract^(0).
  ```

  The fixed-time row passes if an AF-normalized character-domain estimate
  holds:

  ```text
  |u_0^act - exp(-t_i C_2(rho_0)/2)|
    <= K_HK g_i^2 + o(g_i^2).
  ```

  A total-variation estimate of order `g_i^2` is sufficient. The row fails
  if the fixed-time defect divided by `g_i^2` diverges, and `SEL_0` fails
  immediately if the lower defect floor already exceeds `R_0^crit`. Paper 19
  also records the matched-time alternative:

  ```text
  tau_match = -2 log(u_0^time)/C_2(rho_0)
  ```

  removes only the time/scheme debit if `tau_match/g_i^2` remains inside the
  same AF scheme slack and all other records remain same-ledger compatible.
  The non-time residuals
  `K_block^(0)+K_cross^(0)+K_extract^(0)` still have to be paid, so this is a
  proof-coordinate option, not a hidden ontology move. Current source papers
  do not yet prove or falsify the fixed-time `O(g_i^2)` estimate, and they do
  not yet prove that the non-time residual upper budget is below `R_0^crit`.

- Paper 19 has now started proving the four decomposed constants. The exact
  source reduction is:

  ```text
  K_time^(0)   <= (C_2(rho_0)/2) limsup |tau_time-t_i|/g_i^2;
  K_block^(0) <= B_0       from HK-BLOCK-COEFF_0(B_0);
  K_cross^(0) <= C_0^res   from residual exponential decay plus log collar;
  K_extract^(0) <= X_0     from exact/operational coefficient readout.
  ```

  The non-time residual pass budget is

  ```text
  K_NT^up = B_0 + C_0^res + X_0 < R_0^crit.
  ```

  The cross term has a concrete Paper-16 route: if `HK-AN-CLOSE` supplies a
  size-resolved residual envelope with positive
  `Delta_res=mu_res-h_KP-m`, then a collar
  `r_col ~ 2 log(1/g_i)/Delta_res` makes the cross coefficient drift
  `O(g_i^2)`. The extraction term is zero in the exact normalized-character
  readout branch. The hard remaining local source is the same-block
  coefficient gate `HK-BLOCK-COEFF_0(B_0)`, plus the actual numerical
  comparison `B_0+C_0^res+X_0<R_0^crit`.

- Paper 19 has now attacked `HK-BLOCK-COEFF_0(B_0)` itself. The local
  same-block gate is no longer opaque. After the heat-kernel time tangent is
  absorbed into `tau_time`, the paper proves:

  ```text
  finite local coefficient Lipschitz constant L_0^blk
  + transverse local residual A_0^blk = O(g_i^2)
  => B_0 = L_0^blk A_0^blk.
  ```

  The Paper-16 ingredients are identified as `HK-CT-CLOSE`,
  `HK-SF-CLOSE`, `HK-LF-CLOSE`, and `HK-AN-CLOSE`, but the actual
  `SEL_0` constants remain to be computed:

  ```text
  A_0^blk = A_sf,0 + A_ct,0 + A_sch,0 + A_lf,0.
  ```

  The next scalar test is therefore

  ```text
  L_0^blk A_0^blk + C_0^res + X_0 < R_0^crit.
  ```

- Paper 19 has now attacked `L_0^blk` and closed it as a finite local
  record-norm constant. For the one-block exponential-tilt coefficient map,
  the covariance derivative bound gives

  ```text
  L_0^blk <= 2 C_sup,0,
  ```

  where `C_sup,0` is the finite constant by which the declared local
  coefficient norm dominates sup norm. In an exact character-basis norm with
  direct sup domination, `C_sup,0=1`, hence `L_0^blk<=2`. The scalar test is
  now:

  ```text
  2 C_sup,0 A_0^blk + C_0^res + X_0 < R_0^crit.
  ```

  At this point the remaining same-block burden is not the Lipschitz factor;
  it is the transverse residual
  `A_0^blk=A_sf,0+A_ct,0+A_sch,0+A_lf,0`. The first pressure point is the
  local large-field `O(g_i^2)` term.

- Paper 19 has now attacked that local large-field term. In the `SEL_0`
  normalization it proves the reduction

  ```text
  local HK-LF-REP on SEL_0
  + collar-adapted HK-BFE with c_B delta^2>0
  + t_i <= T_+ g_i^2
  => A_lf,0 = 0.
  ```

  The proof uses the Paper-16 large-field mechanism in its sharp local form:
  the supported coefficient representation gives
  `A_lf,j <= M_lf,0 P(E_lf,0,j)`, while the bad-block finite-energy estimate
  gives `P(E_lf,0,j)<=C_B exp(-c_B delta^2/t_i)`. Since `t_i=O(g_i^2)`,
  this is `o(g_i^2)`. The remaining local test is therefore

  ```text
  2 C_sup,0 (A_sf,0 + A_ct,0 + A_sch,0) + C_0^res + X_0 < R_0^crit.
  ```

  Paper 19 has now closed the local large-field source input for this
  `SEL_0` row. It imports same-metric heat constants, proves `COL-EXT_0` for
  the actual block/collar template by constructing a bounded axial-tree right
  inverse and bounding the BCH/Bianchi remainder, chooses
  `0<e_col<c_H/q_loc` and `q_loc(e_col+L_B alpha^2)<a_ad<c_H`, proves the
  finite local `HK-LF-REP-SRC` ledger, and verifies size-one bad-collar
  support on the same record event. Therefore `LF-IMP_0` holds and
  `A_lf,0=0`; after that come the small-field/counterterm/scheme constants.

- Paper 19 has now pushed the remaining transverse residual into a full
  local conditional theorem. It defines:

  ```text
  SF-TRANS_0: finite local small-field expansion with every transverse
              vertex at order g_i^{2p}, p>=1;
  CT-TRANS_0: no unabsorbed relevant/marginal transverse counterterm,
              with remaining counterterm projection O(g_i^2);
  SCH-TRANS_0: matched-scheme first derivative is time-tangent and the
               transverse scheme remainder is quadratic.
  ```

  The resulting constants are

  ```text
  A_sf,0^src = sum_{p_sf,a=1} C_sf,a,
  A_ct,0^src = C_ct,0 if p_ct=1, else 0,
  A_sch,0^src = (1/2) H_sch,0 K_sch,0^2.
  ```

  Paper 19 proves the local row passes if

  ```text
  2 C_sup,0(A_sf,0^src+A_ct,0^src+A_sch,0^src)+C_0^res+X_0<R_0^crit.
  ```

  This is still conditional on the actual source verification, but steps 1-5
  of the same-block attack are now explicit and finite-dimensional.

- Paper 19 has now attacked `SF-TRANS_0` specifically. It introduces the
  finite `SEL_0` small-field vertex ledger `SF-VERT_0` and the neutral
  odd-vertex cancellation gate `SF-ODD_0`. The proved decision is:

  ```text
  SF-VERT_0 + SF-ODD_0 + time-tangent absorption
  => SF-TRANS_0,

  nonzero transverse small-field term of order g_i^q, q<2
  => SF-TRANS_0 is false.
  ```

  The expected Yang-Mills mechanism is favorable: a single cubic order-`g_i`
  insertion is odd and vanishes against the neutral `SEL_0` character battery,
  so the first transverse terms should appear at order `g_i^2`.

- Paper 19 now writes that first `SEL_0` one-block worksheet explicitly. The
  second-order vertex list is

  ```text
  I_sf^(2) = {4,33,J2,gf2,cov2,rec2,norm2},
  ```

  and the small-field debit is computed as

  ```text
  A_sf,0^src =
    C_sf,4+C_sf,33+C_sf,J2+C_sf,gf2
   +C_sf,cov2+C_sf,rec2+C_sf,norm2.
  ```

  The order-`g_i` cubic/odd term vanishes after neutral character pushforward,
  and the order-`g_i^2` heat-kernel time tangent is absorbed into the matched
  time coordinate.

- Paper 19 has now evaluated this seven-constant row symbolically against
  `R_0^crit`. In connected normalization, the chosen axial-tree gauge, and
  the minimal `SEL_0` coefficient readout, the row is:

  ```text
  C_sf,4     <= 24 M_4,0 C_4 C_cov^2,
  C_sf,33    <= 18 M_33,0 C_3^2 C_cov^3,
  C_sf,J2    <= M_J,0 C_J C_cov,
  C_sf,gf2   = 0,
  C_sf,cov2  <= M_cov,0 K_cov,0^blk,
  C_sf,rec2  = 0,
  C_sf,norm2 = 0.
  ```

  The same-block local row passes exactly when the evaluated margin
  `M_loc,0^eval>0`. The remaining work is now the finite source evaluation
  of `M_4,0`, `M_33,0`, `M_J,0`, `M_cov,0`, `K_cov,0^blk`, and the companion
  counterterm/scheme/cross constants.

- Paper 19 has now frozen the strongest minimal same-block normalization:
  connected/cumulant normalization, strict axial-tree chart, exact
  `rho_0` coefficient readout, exact block-conditioned Gaussian as reference,
  and an `ell^1` normalized-character basis. This gives:

  ```text
  X_0 = 0,
  K_cov,0^blk = 0,
  C_sup,0 = 1.
  ```

  The finite projection constants are now computable finite-basis upper sums:

  ```text
  M_a,0 = sum_{b in B_0^perp} limsup_j |m_a,b,j|,
  a in {4,33,J}.
  ```

  Hence the minimal same-block row is:

  ```text
  A_sf,0^min =
    24 M_4,0 C_4 C_cov^2
   +18 M_33,0 C_3^2 C_cov^3
   +M_J,0 C_J C_cov.
  ```

  If no transverse diagnostic records are declared for the same-block
  coefficient source, then `B_0^perp` is empty and `A_sf,0^min=0`. This
  closes steps 1-2 as a finite-basis calculation; the remaining local
  conditions are the counterterm, scheme, and cross-residual debits.

- Paper 19 has now attacked the counterterm debit. In the pure-gauge
  minimal row, relevant/marginal counterterms are time-tangent or fixed by
  the local normalization:

  ```text
  Pi_0^perp R_rel/marg,0^ct = 0.
  ```

  The irrelevant local counterterm remainder contributes

  ```text
  A_ct,0^min <=
    M_ct,0 C_ct(1+3 C_cov^2) C_obs,0,  if p=1,
    0,                                      if p>1.
  ```

  In the coefficient-only minimal row, `B_0^perp` is empty, so
  `M_ct,0=0` and `A_ct,0^min=0`. Any surviving relevant/marginal transverse
  counterterm of order `g_i^q`, `q<2`, falsifies `CT-TRANS_0`. This leaves
  the scheme debit, attacked in the next item.

- Paper 19 has now attacked the scheme debit. After the heat-kernel time
  coordinate is separated, the remaining finite scheme coordinate `lambda_j`
  is tested by

  ```text
  K_sch,0^min = limsup_j ||lambda_j||/g_i,
  H_sch,0^min = finite transverse Hessian norm.
  ```

  If the first derivative is time-tangent or normalization-fixed, then

  ```text
  A_sch,0^min = (1/2) H_sch,0^min (K_sch,0^min)^2.
  ```

  In the time-only minimal branch, `lambda_j=0`; in the coefficient-only
  branch `B_0^perp` is empty. Either way `A_sch,0^min=0`. A surviving
  transverse linear scheme derivative with displacement order `g_i^q`,
  `q<2`, falsifies `SCH-TRANS_0`.

  The fully debited minimal local margin is now

  ```text
  M_loc,0^{min,ct,sch}
   = [(1-chi)(1-epsilon_A)/(1+epsilon_A)] C_2(rho_0)/2
     - C_0^res
     - 2(A_sf,0^min + A_ct,0^min + A_sch,0^min).
  ```

  In the coefficient-only, time-only minimal branch, the local test reduces
  to the single residual inequality

  ```text
  C_0^res
  <
  [(1-chi)(1-epsilon_A)/(1+epsilon_A)] C_2(rho_0)/2.
  ```

- Paper 19 has now reduced this remaining residual inequality to the
  Paper-16 residual-polymer tail. With

  ```text
  Delta_res = mu_res - h_KP - m > 0,
  K_res = C_KP A_res/(1-exp(-Delta_res)),
  C_res^env = limsup_j K_res exp(-Delta_res d_j^av)/g_i^2,
  ```

  the maximal available collar proves

  ```text
  HK-CROSS-COEFF_0(C_res^env).
  ```

  For any target `theta_res<1`, the minimal local row closes if the targeted
  collar

  ```text
  r_j^target =
  ceil( Delta_res^{-1}
        [2 log(1/g_i)
         + log(K_res/(theta_res R_0^crit))] )
  ```

  fits cofinally inside the available window:

  ```text
  r_res <= r_j^target <= d_j^av.
  ```

  The stronger growth-rate route

  ```text
  d_j^av - (2/Delta_res) log(1/g_i) -> +infty
  ```

  makes `C_res^env=0`. If `C_res^env>=R_0^crit`, the present residual-tail
  proof is too weak for this row; an actual lower residual floor at that
  level falsifies the row.

- Paper 19 has now proved the intended residual-tail import and geometry
  pass. Paper 16 Theorem 9N.2A exports, under `HK-AN-CLOSE(m)`,

  ```text
  Delta_res = mu_res - h_KP - m > 0,
  K_res = C_KP A_res/(1-exp(-Delta_res)).
  ```

  The centered square fractional `SEL_0` placement gives

  ```text
  d_j^av >= c_av L_j - b_av,
  0<c_av<(1-alpha)/2.
  ```

  Since `L_j=floor(sqrt(s)g_i^{-1})` while
  `r_j^target=(2/Delta_res)log(1/g_i)+O(1)`, the targeted residual collar
  fits cofinally for every `theta_res<1`. Hence

  ```text
  HK-AN-CLOSE(m) + centered SEL_0
  => C_res^env = 0
  => C_0^res = 0 < R_0^crit
  ```

  on the coefficient-only, time-only minimal local row. The geometry is no
  longer the obstruction. Paper 19 also assembles the dependency-ordered
  clean branch:

  ```text
  coefficient-only MIN-SEL_0
  + HK-SF-YM2 on the same SEL_0 record law
  + Theorem 8J.15M.1 local large-field import
  + pure-gauge counterterm ledger
  + time-only scheme branch
  + HK-AN-CLOSE(m)
  + centered square SEL_0 geometry
  => A_sf,0^min=A_lf,0=A_ct,0^min=A_sch,0^min=X_0=C_0^res=0
  => M_loc,0^clean=R_0^crit>0.
  ```

  Equivalently, the minimal same-block scalar debit is zero on the exported
  record law:

  ```text
  2 C_sup,0(A_sf,0^min+A_ct,0^min+A_sch,0^min)+C_0^res+X_0=0,
  M_loc,0^clean=R_0^crit>0.
  ```

  The remaining source burden is proving Paper 16 `HK-AN-SRC(m)`, hence
  `HK-AN-CLOSE(m)`, with actual compatible constants. Paper 16 now also
  closes the standard finite-template global `HK-LF-CLOSE` source by Theorem
  9J.8, while Paper 19 closes the local `SEL_0` large-field import by
  Theorem 8J.15M.1. Paper 16 also proves
  `HK-CT-RATE => HK-CT-SRC => HK-CT-CLOSE => HK-CTS`; on the clean minimal
  counterterm row the nonlocal counterterm/scheme tail amplitudes are zero,
  while any non-clean convention must pass the same-record finite rate
  audit. Paper 16 also proves `HK-AN-RES-COMMON`, so once those source
  constants are fixed the common residual constants are assembled
  automatically. Paper 16 now packages the clean finite-template analytic
  branch as `HK-AN-FINTPL-CLOSE(m)`. Paper 19 now closes the executable
  same-record import audit `P19-AN-AUDIT(m)` on the clean coefficient-only
  `SEL_0` branch: the finite row data
  `Delta_B,L_ent,L_KP,lambda_D,R_blk,C_v^{row},r_res^clean,m` are attached
  to the same heat-kernel row, and the residual-decoration battery is included
  in the Paper-16 residual KP battery with `D_sub=1`. Thus
  `P19-AN-IMPORT(m)` holds, and Paper 19 imports one named analytic
  certificate instead of reconstructing the KP worksheet.

- Paper 19 now has a final AF-matched direct-witness closure theorem. With

  ```text
  A_AFM^* = (1+chi)s_+ C_2(rho)/2 + s_+R_H/(1-r_*),
  B_AFM^* = (1-chi)s_- C_2(rho)/2 - s_+R_H,
  Sig_AFM = exp(-n_+ A_AFM^*)[1-exp(-q_- B_AFM^*)],
  ```

  the direct-witness branch proves `c_15^tail>0` if

  ```text
  B_AFM^* > 0
  and
  L_AFM^sharp
    := limsup_j(Delta_dec,j^bd + T_loss,j^bd)
    < Sig_AFM
  ```

  cofinally on the same tower. It is falsified by AF area mismatch,
  coefficient-window failure, or loss dominance. This means Paper 19 is now
  complete as a conditional source-constant decision paper, but actual
  `4D SU(N)` confinement remains conditional until the two actual estimates
  are proved:

  ```text
  R_H^opt < R_H^crit,
  L_AFM^sharp < Sig_AFM.
  ```

- The direct-witness loss budget has now been reduced to an exact
  prove/falsify gate. Paper 19 defines:

  ```text
  eta_dec,j^bd = eta_res,j^bd + C_ch,j Tail_CE,j,
  Delta_dec,j^bd
    <= exp(c_Delta^* eta_*/(1-eta_*))-1,
  T_loss,j^bd = T_11,j+T_12,j+T_13,j+T_14,j.
  ```

  The full direct-witness reserve passes if:

  ```text
  P19-DW-THETA(Theta_*)
  + P19-DW-PHI(Phi_*)
  + limsup eta_dec,j^bd <= eta_* < 1
  + limsup c_Delta,j^* <= c_Delta^*
  + limsup T_loss,j^bd <= T_*
  + exp(-Theta_*)(1-exp(-Phi_*))
    > exp(c_Delta^* eta_*/(1-eta_*))-1 + T_*
  => c_15^tail > 0.
  ```

  Equivalently, with explicit source constants, the loss side passes when

  ```text
  eta_* = eta_res^* + eta_ch^* < 1,
  exp(c_Delta^* eta_*/(1-eta_*)) - 1
    + T_11^*+T_12^*+T_13^*+T_14^*
  < Sig_AFM.
  ```

  Paper 19 now names the first two loss-source audits:

  ```text
  P19-CHTAIL-AUDIT(eta_ch^*),
  P19-CDELTA-AUDIT(c_Delta^*).
  ```

  The character-tail audit is now closed on the clean branch by the
  heat-kernel Weyl-Casimir cutoff schedule: for any
  `eta_ch^*<1-eta_19^res`, choose `R_j` cofinally so that
  `limsup C_ch,j Tail_CE,j<=eta_ch^*`; the canonical half-margin choice is
  `eta_ch^*=(1-eta_19^res)/2`. Paper 19 now also closes
  `P19-CDELTA-AUDIT(c_Delta^*)` on the centered square thick `SEL_0` branch:
  the finite-template decoration geometry gives
  `c_Delta^*=C_xi^SEL0+C_xip^SEL0`. Thus
  `Delta_dec^bd <= exp(c_Delta^* eta_*/(1-eta_*))-1` in limsup.

  Paper 19 now also decomposes the four transport ceilings into component
  audits:

  ```text
  P19-T11-AUDIT(T_11^*):
    local-RG + RP + covariance + gauge reconstruction;
  P19-T12-AUDIT(T_12^*):

  P19-T13-AUDIT(T_13^*):
  ```

  The component source packages prove the transport gate by limsup

  ```text
  P19-T11-SRC + P19-T12-SRC + P19-T13-SRC + P19-T14-SRC
  => P19-DW-TLOSS(T_*),
  T_* = T_11^*+T_12^*+T_13^*+T_14^*.
  ```

  Paper 19 now closes the common-record transport audit and the Paper-14

  ```text
  P19-TOWER + HK-WP-CLOSE + same-battery Paper-14 export
  => P19-TR-COMMON,

  P19-TR-COMMON + P19-P14-EXPORT(E_14^*)
  ```

  Paper 19 now also gives the reduced same-record ledgers for the remaining

  ```text
  P19-T11-LEDGER
  ```

  Therefore the final source comparison is now the single scalar test:

  ```text
  exp(c_Delta^* eta_*/(1-eta_*)) - 1
  + A_11^loc+A_11^RP+A_11^Cov+A_11^gauge
  + A_12^per+A_12^cusp+A_12^smear+A_12^app
  + A_13^surf+A_13^entry+A_13^exact
  ```

  Passing this proves the AF-matched direct-witness loss budget. Failing to

  Paper 19 now freezes this as the final source worksheet
  `P19-FINAL-SRC-WORKSHEET` and begins the first component attack. The local

  ```text
  P19-T11-LOC-AF(A_11^loc)
  <= weighted Paper-11 AF tail
     + weighted finite-precision tail.
  ```

  Explicitly, Paper 11 AF.11/AF.14 give the source bound

  ```text
  A_11^loc,AF =
    limsup_j sum_{k>=j} L_j^rec 2 e^alpha G_k Q_k^* exp(-mu R_k),
  A_11^loc = A_11^loc,AF + A_11^prec.
  ```

  If these weighted tails vanish, then `A_11^loc=0`. Paper 19 now also

  ```text
  P19-T11-RP(A_11^RP):
    HK-RP-LEDGER + RP half of HK-RPCOV-CLOSE;
  ```

  These attacks pay the projective, regulator/chart, block/collar,

  ```text
  P19-T11-LOC-AF
  + P19-T11-RP
  ```

  The reduction is still scalar and conditional: the actual cofinal limsups

  Paper 19 now also attacks the `T_12` loop-readout bucket in the correct
  reduced order:

  ```text
  perimeter/cusp counterterm tails
  -> smearing-removal tail
  -> loop-approximant/readout tail.
  ```

  The named source attacks are:

  ```text
  P19-T12-SMEAR(A_12^smear),
  ```

  They use Paper 12's connected perimeter/cusp decomposition, local

  ```text
  P19-T12-PC
  + P19-T12-SMEAR

  => P19-T12-LEDGER

     <= A_12^per+A_12^cusp+A_12^smear+A_12^app.
  ```

  ```text
  A_12^per   = limsup_j sum_{k>=j} eta_perLC,j,k,
  ```

  The zero branch is also explicit: if the perimeter/cusp calibration tails,

  Paper 19 now also attacks `T_13`, the hardest dynamical bucket. The order is
  deliberately:

  ```text
  prove B_C u_{rho,s0}<1 cofinally
  -> bound A_13^surf
  -> prove exact-entry transport A_13^entry
  -> prove cutoff-to-exact scalar comparison A_13^exact.
  ```

  The named gates are:

  ```text
  P19-T13-SUB(q_13^*),
  P19-T13-ENTRY(A_13^entry),
  P19-T13-EXACT(A_13^exact).
  ```

  Paper 19 now evaluates the first dynamical gate by the scalar limsup

  ```text
  q_13^act =
    limsup_j max_C D_C,j E_C,j^surf u_{rho,s0,j}.
  ```

  The exact decision is:

  ```text
  q_13^act < 1
  <=> P19-T13-SUB(q_13^*) for some q_13^*<1.
  ```
