  If `q_13^act>=1`, the surface-polymer route fails at the named
  subcriticality gate. Paper 19 also gives the logarithmic margin form:

  ```text
  liminf_j (kappa_sheet,j - max_C(log D_C,j+log E_C,j^surf)) > 0
  => q_13^act < 1.
  ```

  Paper 16 `HK-SURF-CLOSE` imports this margin when its surface reserve is
  verified on the same scalar record tower. Paper 19 now also attacks the
  three source factors separately:

  ```text
  P19-T13-ESURF(h_13^*)   : finite-degree surface entropy,
  P19-T13-DEC(d_13^*)     : decoration growth per excess plaquette,
  P19-T13-LEAD(kappa_13^*): leading central character coefficient.
  ```

  The first component is now closed on the reduced `4D` hypercubic
  block-surface template:

  ```text
  Delta_plaq^4D = 20,
  R_loc^4D = 1,
  h_13^* = 3 + log 20.
  ```

  If one uses an orientation-doubled support convention, the fallback is
  `h_13^*=3+log 40`. The default reduced-support branch uses `3+log 20`.

  The second component is now closed from the same-record decoration audits:

  ```text
  d_13^* = C_xi eta_*/(1-eta_*),
  eta_* = eta_19^res + eta_ch^*.
  ```

  On the centered square `SEL_0` branch with the canonical half-margin
  character cutoff,

  ```text
  d_13^SEL0 = C_xi^SEL0 (1+eta_19^res)/(1-eta_19^res).
  ```

  This deliberately uses only the area-charged collar multiplicity `C_xi`.
  The endpoint/corner constant `C_xip` stays in `Delta_dec`; it is not
  double-charged inside the surface ratio `D_C`.

  The third component now has a frozen same-record coefficient target and an
  exact coefficient-window decision:

  ```text
  k_rho,j = <K_p,j,chi_rho>/<chi_rho,chi_rho>,
  kappa_13^CE = liminf_j -log k_rho,j,
  epsilon_13^CE = limsup_j sum_{lambda != 0,rho} d_lambda |k_lambda,j|.
  ```

  If `kappa_13^CE>0` and `epsilon_13^CE<infinity`, then every strict
  `0<kappa_13^*<kappa_13^CE` and `epsilon_ch>epsilon_13^CE` closes
  `P19-T13-CEWIN`, hence closes `P19-T13-LEAD(kappa_13^*)` and Paper 13
  `CE(s_0,rho,L)` on the same finite battery. Paper 19 now executes the
  six-step attack:

  ```text
  identify K_p,j
  -> test 0<k_rho,j<1
  -> test kappa_13^CE>0
  -> test epsilon_13^CE<infinity
  -> audit same-record debits
  -> apply the exact CEWIN decision.
  ```

  The first, fourth, fifth, and sixth items are closed: the target marginal is fixed,
  the finite heat-kernel source rows give a central `L^1` density with
  Peter-Weyl coefficients for `K_p,j`, the non-leading CE tail is bounded by
  the same `P19-CHTAIL-AUDIT` used by `P19-T13-DEC`, double charging is
  excluded, and the pass/fail theorem is exact. The second and third items now have proved
  same-target reference-defect/reference-gap/log-margin routes:

  ```text
  delta_sign,j/u_ref,j < 1 cofinally
  => k_rho,j>0 cofinally.

  delta_sign,j/(1-u_ref,j) < 1 cofinally
  => k_rho,j<1 cofinally.

  same-target sign + limsup_j (u_ref,j + delta_sign,j) < 1
  => kappa_13^CE>0.

  AF-matched same-target rate test:
  liminf_j (a_j - log(1+r_j)) > 0.

  If the selected same-target branch instead has `u_ref,j -> 1` and
  `delta_sign,j -> 0`, then `k_rho,j -> 1` and `kappa_13^CE = 0`; that
  branch cannot supply the `T_13` surface suppression.

  P19-CHTAIL-AUDIT(eta_ch^*) on the P19-T13-DEC ledger
  => epsilon_13^CE <= eta_ch^* < infinity.
  ```

  The actual same-target leading defect and log-margin estimates remain
  unsupplied. The fourth item is not a separate hidden cutoff: it is paid by
  the declared character-tail/decorrelation ledger, giving
  `epsilon_13^CE<=eta_ch^*<infinity`. Current source papers define the Haar
  projection and prove the consequences of the coefficient window, but do
  not yet give an unconditional numerical leading projection estimate for
  actual `4D SU(N)`.

  These assemble to the component margin

  ```text
  mu_13^comp = kappa_13^* - d_13^* - h_13^*.
  ```

  If `mu_13^comp>0`, then

  ```text
  q_13^act <= exp(-mu_13^comp) < 1.
  ```

  If `mu_13^comp<=0`, this component route is inconclusive unless the exact
  `q_13^act` is shown to be at least one. With the finite surface envelope

  ```text
  M_13^surf =
    limsup_j max_C A_C,j exp(xi'_C,j) u_{rho,s0,j}^{N_j(C)},
  ```

  Paper 19 proves the surface-tail estimate

  ```text
  A_13^surf >= M_13^surf q_13^*/(1-q_13^*).
  ```

  The final reduced dynamical ledger is:

  ```text
  P19-T13-SUB
  + finite surface envelope
  + P19-T13-ENTRY
  + P19-T13-EXACT
  + P19-TR-COMMON
  => P19-T13-LEDGER
  => limsup T_13,j <= A_13^surf+A_13^entry+A_13^exact.
  ```

  This is where the real nonperturbative confinement content sits. The route
  now depends on Paper 13's exact-entry chain:
  `BC, CE, RPF, KP_dec, SUB, WP => ACSB => SB => surface-polymer entry =>
  exact RG entry => RSB`. Failure of any one of these gates is a named
  obstruction, not a hidden error term.

  The sufficient AF-matched loss gate fails if
  `L_AFM^sharp >= Sig_AFM`; an actual direct-witness falsification needs the
  stronger comparison of a lower loss floor with an upper signal ceiling.
  Current source papers define these quantities and prove conditional
  compatibility, but do not yet supply the sharp cofinal constants needed to
  prove or falsify the loss budget on the actual `4D SU(N)` tower.

## V3 Paper 20: Actual Heat-Kernel Coefficient And Loss Estimates

Suggested title:

`Actual Heat-Kernel Coefficient And Loss Estimates For 4D SU(N) Direct-Witness Confinement`

Draft:

`relativistic-isp-v3-paper20-actual-heat-kernel-coefficient-loss-estimates.md`

Main question:

> Do the actual `4D SU(N)` heat-kernel source constants left open by Paper 19
> satisfy the two strict scalar inequalities needed for the Paper-18/Paper-19
> direct-witness confinement closure?

Main job:

- freeze one common AF-matched selector/tower before any estimate is made;
- prove or falsify the same-record coefficient estimate

  ```text
  R_H^opt < R_H^crit;
  ```

- prove or falsify the same-record loss estimate

  ```text
  L_AFM^sharp < Sig_AFM;
  ```

- keep the leading coefficient, decoration, transport, and surface-entry
  ledgers on the same pushed-forward scalar record law;
- import Paper 19 only as a conditional closure theorem and obstruction
  ledger, not as a source of the missing constants.

Pass condition:

- a single frozen selector satisfying both strict inequalities above. Then
  Paper 19 imports Paper 18 and closes the AF-matched direct-witness
  confinement branch.

Fail condition:

- either strict inequality fails on the frozen selector, or every admissible
  selector fails one of them. In that case Paper 20 records the exact scalar
  obstruction: coefficient error, loss dominance, surface-entry failure, or
  selector inadmissibility.

Why this matters:

Paper 19 is complete as a conditional source-constant decision paper. It
cannot honestly declare an unconditional proof until the two actual estimates
above are proved on the same whole-process tower. Paper 20 is therefore not a
synthesis paper; it is the source-estimate paper.

Planned structure:

1. **Honest boundary and imports.** Import from Paper 19 only the exact
   conditional closure:

   ```text
   R_H^opt < R_H^crit
   + L_AFM^sharp < Sig_AFM
   => direct-witness confinement closure.
   ```

2. **Common tower and selector freeze.** Fix the AF trajectory, heat-kernel
   row, block scale, thick/co-scaling windows, `rho`, `chi`, `epsilon_A`,
   character cutoff, counterterm convention, and pushed-forward scalar
   record law before estimating any constant.
3. **Anti-circularity audit.** Verify that the frozen selector contains only
   structural tower/readout/debit data and does not already assume
   `R_H^opt<R_H^crit`, `L_AFM^sharp<Sig_AFM`, a Wilson-loop area law, or a
   mass gap. In Paper 20 this is the named audit `P20-NOSMUGGLE`.
4. **Same-record coefficient estimates.** Prove or falsify
   `R_H^opt<R_H^crit` by bounding the heat-kernel coefficient defect after
   block readout, projection, chart/counterterm convention, finite-volume
   passage, and RG drift:

   ```text
   K_HK + K_proj + K_chart + K_ct + K_vol + K_tail < R_H^crit.
   ```

5. **Decoration and character-tail constants.** Re-evaluate
   `eta_res^*`, `eta_ch^*`, and `c_Delta^*` on the frozen selector and test
   the decoration debit

   ```text
   D_dec^* = exp(c_Delta^* eta_*/(1-eta_*)) - 1.
   ```

6. **Non-surface transport ceilings.** Evaluate `T_11^*`, `T_12^*`, and
   `T_14^*`, keeping projective/regulator/volume/readout charges disjoint.
7. **Surface/entry dynamical ceiling.** Evaluate `T_13^*` through
   subcriticality, surface tail, exact-entry transport, and cutoff-to-exact
   scalar comparison. This is the hardest nonperturbative confinement part.
   The active `SEL2` reduction now names the sharp remaining rate gate:

   ```text
   P20-SEL2-TREE-RATE-GATE:
   q_rho gamma_rho > Theta_esc^tree,
   T_-^{SEL2} > Theta_T^tree(rho).
   ```

   Papers 11 and 12 do not supply this gate. Paper 11 supplies RG residual
   and perturbative trajectory ledgers; Paper 12 supplies renormalized
   Wilson-loop readout control. The tree-rate gate is a same-record
   block-plaquette coefficient source for Paper 20 or a later source paper.
8. **Final scalar optimization.** Test

   ```text
   D_dec^* + T_11^* + T_12^* + T_13^* + T_14^* < Sig_AFM.
   ```

9. **Closure or falsification ledger.** If both headline inequalities pass,
   close the Paper-19/Paper-18 branch. If not, record the exact scalar
   obstruction.

Current Paper-20 status after the Paper 11--12 audits:

```text
coefficient/loss architecture: reduced to explicit same-record scalar gates;
P20-SEL2-TREE-RATE-GATE: parked active obstruction;
unconditional actual 4D SU(N) confinement: not proved.
```

Paper 20 is now closed as a conditional/reduction paper. Its handoff is to a
new source paper dedicated to the parked tree-rate obstruction.

## V3 Paper 21: SEL2 Tree-Rate Source Or Falsification

Suggested title:

`SEL2 Tree-Rate Source Or Falsification For 4D SU(N) Direct-Witness Confinement`

Draft:

`relativistic-isp-v3-paper21-sel2-tree-rate-source-falsification.md`

Main question:

> On the frozen same-record `SEL2` branch left by Paper 20, can the normalized
> block-plaquette sheet rate beat the rooted surface-polymer entropy, or is the
> `SEL2` route structurally too expensive?

Main job:

- inherit Paper 20's frozen `SEL2` selector, no-smuggling audit, decoration
  pass, transport ledger, scalar coefficient source, and rooted surface-growth
  threshold;
- decide the time half

  ```text
  P20-SEL2-TREE-TIME(rho):
  T_-^{SEL2} > Theta_T^tree(rho);
  ```

- decide the escape half

  ```text
  P20-SEL2-ESC-MASS(V_rho,gamma_rho,q_rho):
  q_rho gamma_rho > Theta_esc^tree;
  ```

- if both pass, evaluate the surface prefactor cap

  ```text
  M_13^{surf,SEL2}
  <
  underline M_pre13^{SEL2,20}
  (exp(Delta_13,tree^{SEL2})-1);
  ```

- if either fails, record an exact falsification of the strict reduced `SEL2`
  route without claiming that all possible confinement strategies fail;
- if both remain too expensive, investigate a same-record surface-growth
  theorem that lowers `Theta_esc^tree` and `Theta_T^tree`.

Pass condition:

```text
P20-SEL2-TREE-TIME
+ P20-SEL2-ESC-MASS
+ prefactor cap
=> Paper-20 SEL2 loss pass on the frozen strict branch.
```

Fail condition:

- `T_clean,+^{SEL2}<=Theta_T^tree(rho)` for the frozen selector;
- same-target normalized collapse makes every fixed escape window vanish;
- the strongest available escape product stays below `Theta_esc^tree`;
- the prefactor cap fails even after the rate gate passes.

Why this matters:

Paper 20 already proved the coefficient/debit architecture and named the final
rate obstruction. Paper 21 decides whether that obstruction is a missing source
estimate, a surface-entropy overcount, or a genuine failure of the strict
`SEL2` direct-witness route.

Planned structure:

1. **Imports and boundary.** Import Paper 20 only as a frozen same-record
   reduction. Do not import a Wilson-loop area law, mass gap, or continuum
   Yang-Mills existence theorem.
2. **Frozen constants.** Restate `Theta_esc^tree`, `Theta_T^tree`,
   `T_clean,-^{SEL2}`, `T_clean,+^{SEL2}`,
   `underline M_pre13^{SEL2,20}`, and `M_13^{surf,SEL2}`.
3. **Time gate.** Use Paper 20's trichotomy:

   ```text
   T_clean,- > Theta_T^tree => pass;
   T_clean,+ <= Theta_T^tree => falsify;
   otherwise sharpen selector or park.
   ```

4. **Escape gate.** Prove a near-maximal anti-concentration source, prove
   collapse, or show the rooted surface threshold must be lowered.
5. **Surface-growth fallback.** If `ESC-MASS` is too strong, replace the
   rooted tree bound by a sharper same-record surface-connective theorem and
   rerun the two thresholds.
6. **Prefactor cap.** Only after the rate gate passes, test the remaining
   `M_13^{surf,SEL2}` inequality.
7. **Outcome theorem.** Pass, falsification, or conditional handoff.

Current Paper-21 status after the final source-table audit:

```text
structural row maps R_fus, R_act, R_SD, R_cmp: printed;
current licensed support-growing pass graph: empty;
SDSRC+: scalar/projected-envelope audit closed, parked at inverse/projection;
ACTSRC+: finite-envelope audit closed, parked at inverse/admissibility;
CMPSRC+: structural row map printed, source values/inverses still parked;
reduced-tail/confinement conclusion: not proved.
```

Paper 21 is therefore frozen as a source-audit and obstruction ledger. Its
handoff is not a global synthesis but a continuation paper whose first tasks
were `COMMON-INVADM`, `CMPSRC+`, and the licensed pass graph. Paper 22 has now
closed `COMMON-INVADM+` by a row-complete finite scalar-record quotient
construction and closed `CMPSRC+` by a finite same-record comparison-envelope
package. It has also rebuilt the licensed pass graph on the strict envelope
branch and proved finite-depth reduced-tail closure by the support-cardinality
rank. The active obstruction is therefore no longer `CMPVAL+` or
`LICGRAPH+`; it is the upstream Paper-20/Paper-21 tree-rate source gate.

## V3 Paper 22: Continuum Yang-Mills Confinement Continuation

Suggested title:

`Continuum Yang-Mills Confinement Continuation After The SEL2 Source Audit`

Draft:

`relativistic-isp-v3-paper22-continuum-yang-mills-confinement-continuation.md`

Main question:

> After Paper 21's finite source audit, can the strict `SEL2` route print a
> licensed reduced pass graph or prove direct reduced-tail decay without
> importing confinement, a mass gap, or an existing continuum Yang-Mills
> measure?

Main job:

- import Paper 21 Section 130 as the frozen source-audit export ledger;
- use the Paper-22 row-complete finite scalar-record quotient certificate for
  common same-shell inverse/admissibility across `ACTSRC+`, `SDSRC+`, and
  `CMPSRC+`;
- use the Paper-22 finite comparison-envelope certificate
  `P22-CMPSRC-CLOSE+`, with `A_cmp,pass^22 <= 2` on the strict
  unit-normalized no-extra-normal-form branch;
- use the Paper-22 licensed graph certificate `P22-LICGRAPH-CLOSE+`, whose
  support-cardinality rank gives finite maximum path depth
  `K_max^22 <= 81`;
- export the finite-depth reduced-tail closure
  `T_{>=K}^{red,act,22}(j)=0` for `K>K_max^22`;
- freeze the post-Work-III tree-rate worksheet: `TREE-TIME` is the scalar
  selector-time pass/fail test against `Theta_T^tree(rho)`, and `ESC-MASS`
  requires a near-maximal fixed-set weak-tail certificate
  `q_rho gamma_rho>Theta_esc^tree`;
- replace blind escape-set search by the cofinal escape-ceiling functional
  `E_rho^{cof,SEL2}`; the escape half passes exactly when this functional
  beats `Theta_esc^tree`;
- return the remaining obstruction to the Paper-20/Paper-21 tree-rate source
  gate and the associated surface prefactor comparison.

Pass condition:

- `P22-LICGRAPH-CLOSE+` and the finite-depth reduced-tail closure hold on the
  strict envelope branch, so the Paper-22 finite-table obstruction is
  discharged without importing confinement.

Fail condition:

- no Paper-22 finite-table failure occurs on the strict row-complete envelope
  branch, because the rebuilt graph is finite-depth. A failure verdict can only
  reappear if a later branch rejects the strict envelope or finite-battery
  conventions and the rebuilt graph then fails its reduced-tail audit. Such a
  failure would falsify that source route, not confinement itself.

Park condition:

- the strict action envelope, minimal `SD` projection convention, or
  row-complete finite battery is rejected. Then the relevant package must be
  restored as a named park condition and the licensed graph rebuilt. On the
  strict branch, these are no longer live parks.

```text
  SURFLOG is reduced to P22-BRANCHA-XIPLOG(theta_xi) plus optional fixed minimal-area amplifier P22-BRANCHA-AREA(n0), with closure condition theta_xi < (2/3)(n0+1);
  PREDEBIT is reduced to disjoint margin sources P22-BRANCHA-RPCOV-MARGIN(lambda_11) and P22-BRANCHA-RPF-MARGIN(lambda_13), with lambda_11+lambda_13<M_*;
  pure finite-template geometry contributes only O(1) when the Creutz template is fixed; the unprinted surface growth is the decoration/minimal-collar log term Xi'_N and any deliberate battery-template change;
P22-BRANCHB-SURF-AUDIT: Paper 22 Section 40 settles Branch B at the current-corpus level;
  the current rooted-tree surface constant 1+log19 is far above the F4 heat-kernel-tail rescue target G_B<1.427116...;
  the old 1/8 escape source cannot be rescued by any full-support same-boundary surface theorem because cube-bump tubes force G_B>=(log2)/4>log(8/7);
  Branch B reopens only through a new positive full-support theorem P22-BRANCHB-SURF-SHARP(G_B).
P22-BRANCHC-SIGNED-SELECTOR-AUDIT: Paper 22 Section 41 settles Branch C at the current-corpus level;
  Paper 13/19 SUB is an absolute positive surface-polymer theorem and cannot be reused unchanged after support deletion or signed cancellation;
  fixed F4 scalar selectors are heat-kernel limited by Section 29;
  Branch C reopens only through P22-BRANCHC-DECL+EXACTID+EFFSURF(G_C,M_C)+ANCHORPASS.
Branch-A Paper-22 current-corpus verdict: Branch A is complete as a source
audit, not an unconditional confinement proof; active continuation requires
proving P22-BRANCHA-4096-PREFCAP or the adaptive XIPLOG+AREA+RPCOV/RPF margin
package. Paper 23 subsequently closes the adaptive surface side, closes the
RP/Cov transport predebit by an explicit cofinal diagonal-shell selector, and
sharpens the remaining adaptive package to the single exact-entry source gate
`P23-RPF-TRANS0`. Because Branch B and Branch C are both parked behind new
theorem packages, the current continuation should either prove or falsify this
same-law connected-cumulant factorization gate before global synthesis.
```

Why this matters:

Paper 21 did not leave a vague "large constant" problem. It left a concrete
same-record source/pass-graph problem. Paper 22 must not skip over that work
into a global synthesis. The synthesis role is postponed until the continuum
Yang-Mills confinement branch is either closed, falsified on the strict route,
or parked at an irreducible named source theorem.

`Adaptive Branch A Source Campaign For Continuum Yang-Mills Confinement`

  `P23-RPF-MIN-SIGNED-EXT(Theta,omega) + P23-RPF-MIN-KTAIL(kappa)`
  (sufficiently, `P23-RPF-MIN-SIGNED-DUAL(Theta,omega) + MIN-KTAIL(kappa)`)
  with

  where the common `MIN-KTAIL` factor must itself be sourced by exact

  `P23-RPF-MIN-SIGNED-FULL(Theta,omega)`;
  or the older anchored mixed theorem
  `P23-RPF-MIN-ANCHMIX(D,kappa)` with
  $$
  \sinh((2D+D^2/4)/2)+\kappa<
  {e^{-h_{path}}\over1+B_{edge}C_{path}/4},
  $$
  or, less sharply, the mixed-line theorem
  `P23-RPF-MIN-MIXLINE(D,omega,kappa)` with
  $$
  \sinh((2D+\omega^2/4)/2)+\kappa<
  {e^{-h_{path}}\over1+B_{edge}C_{path}/4},
  $$
  or, more sharply, `P23-RPF-MIN-DCENTER(Theta,omega,kappa)` with
  $$
  \sinh((\Theta+\omega^2/4)/2)+\kappa<
  {e^{-h_{path}}\over1+B_{edge}C_{path}/4},
  $$
  or, less sharply, `P23-RPF-MIN-SINK(Theta)` with
  $$
  \sinh(\Theta/2)+\kappa<
  {e^{-h_{path}}\over1+B_{edge}C_{path}/4},
  $$
  or the finite Peter-Weyl package
  `P23-RPF-MIN-MARG-PW(L,delta_tail,kappa)` plus
  \(\Delta_{m,0,L}\le\Delta_L\) with
  $$
  \sinh((\Delta_L+2\delta_{tail})/2)+\kappa<
  {e^{-h_{path}}\over1+B_{edge}C_{path}/4},
  $$
  or, more conservatively, the literal atom-sum source
  \(\overline\Omega_0^{N,j}\le\overline\Omega_*\) with
  $$
  \sinh(3\overline\Omega_*/2)+\kappa<
  {e^{-h_{path}}\over1+B_{edge}C_{path}/4},
  $$
  together with the exact edge-path package; equivalently one may prove
  `P23-RPF-EDGE-SPEC + P23-RPF-EDGE-PATH`, or else a direct screened
  conditional influence estimate `P23-RPF-SCREEN-COND` on the adaptive row.
  The separator package is now parked as a future-source branch,
  reopenable only by a new admissible
  scalar separator record and exact clique identity; off the exact-CE branch the
  central-entry/readout debit must be restored. This is not an unconditional
  confinement proof and not a falsification of the actual branch;
- Paper-19's clean `SEL_0` decoration pass was not spent on the adaptive
  high-alpha `SEL2` row by analogy; Paper 23 Section 11 supplies a separate
  same-record adaptive cutoff construction.

Main question:

> Can the high-\(\alpha\), large-\(N\), same-record Branch-A route close the
> Paper-20 surface prefactor gate by proving the adaptive
> `XIPLOG+AREA+RPCOV/RPF` source package isolated in Paper 22?

Main job:

- import Paper 22 Theorems 38.4, 39.5, 39.7, and 39.8 as the exact adaptive
  Branch-A closure theorem;
- freeze the same high-\(\alpha\) large-\(N\) row family and no-smuggling
  contract;
- prove or falsify `P22-BRANCHA-XIPLOG(theta_xi)`, the uniform
  decoration/minimal-collar logarithmic growth source;
- decide whether the default area floor \(n_0=1\) is sufficient or whether a
  declared fixed-template area amplifier `P22-BRANCHA-AREA(n0)` is needed;
- close RP/Cov using the explicit cofinal diagonal-shell selector and then
  isolate the remaining exact-entry factorization source
  `P23-RPF-TRANS0`;
- close adaptive Branch A if

  ```math
  \theta_\xi<{2\over3}(n_0+1),
  \qquad
  \lambda_{13}<M_*,
  ```

  after Section 12 has set \(\lambda_{11}=0\) by the diagonal RP/Cov selector.

Pass condition:

- the adaptive surface gates and the diagonal RP/Cov selector hold on the same
  pushed-forward `SEL2` law, and the remaining exact-entry factorization
  ceiling satisfies \(\lambda_{13}<M_*\). Paper 23 Sections 13--17 prove this
  cannot be derived from the closed source package alone; it requires a new
  same-law RPF KP/cumulant theorem.  Section 17 shows that the scalar part
  would pass under the clean finite-template identification package
  `P23-RPF-CLEAN-FINTPL-ID + P23-RPF-CLEAN-ROWDATA`; Section 18 sharpens the
  identification half to `P23-RPF-CLEAN-DICT(lambda_RPF)`, and Section 19
  sharpens that dictionary to `P23-RPF-CLEAN-ROWMAP(lambda_RPF)` on the
  printed survivor table. Section 20 executes that map into exact row identity,
  label cover, finite surcharge, and active rowdata. Section 21 audits exact
  row identity componentwise and reduces the nonlocal live part, on the
  exact-CE branch, to `P23-RPF-ROWID-RES`. Section 22 proves that this
  residual-coefficient identity is not supplied by Paper 16's envelope and
  finite-counting theorems. Section 23 closes coefficient identity by using
  the canonical anchored finite coefficient gauge on the same adaptive scalar
  law. Section 24 proves a finite coarse entropy bound but shows that the pass
  condition now needs a sharp canonical automaton/selector entropy bound plus
  active rowdata KP margin. Section 25 prints the structural automaton and
  reduces the sharpness problem to a finite value-local table for the actual
  Möbius nonzero predicate. Section 26 proves the exact rowwise value table
  exists and reduces the useful cofinal table to
  `P23-RPF-HLOC + P23-RPF-HVAL`. Section 27 shows that HVAL is finite algebra
  after HLOC; the primary live source is cofinal bounded HLOC, followed by
  active row data and the scalar KP margin.

Fail condition:

- either the log-growth source necessarily violates
  \(\theta_\xi<2(n_0+1)/3\) for every admissible fixed-template area amplifier,
  or the RPF predebit reaches the actual same-record loss floor
  \(\underline M_{loss}^{SEL2,20}\). A lower floor
  \(\lambda_{13}\ge M_*\) only defeats the imported \(M_*\)-floor sufficient
  test unless an upper ceiling on the actual loss floor is also supplied. This
  falsifies adaptive Branch A, not every confinement strategy.

Park condition:

$$
\mathrm{P23\text{-}RPF\text{-}MIN\text{-}BRIDGEDAMP}(D)
+

## V3 Paper 30: Actual-Law Signed/Bridge Amplitude Or Floor Campaign

Suggested title:

`Actual-Law Signed/Bridge Amplitude Or Floor Campaign`

Draft:

`relativistic-isp-v3-paper30-actual-law-signed-bridge-amplitude-or-floor-campaign.md`

Current status:

- Paper 30 is completed as the signed/bridge continuation forced by
  Paper 29's completion certificate.
- It stays on the actual adaptive `SEL2` pushed-forward scalar law and
  explicitly forbids heat-kernel replacement, hidden Markov bridges,
  independent bridge processes, and continuum Yang-Mills substitution.
- It freezes the actual signed true-bridge Hamiltonian
  \(W_{br,0}^{anc,N,j}\), its doubly centered signed range
  \(\Theta_{br,0}^{N,j}\), and one-line width \(\omega_{br,0}^{N,j}\).
- It proves that `P30-SIGNED-BRIDGE-VALUE(Theta,omega,kappa)` activates the
  Paper-23 signed gate whenever
  $$
  \Theta+\omega^2/4<M_{\mathrm{sgn}}(\kappa).
  $$
- It proves that direct same-law signed values, a narrowed-body finite dual
  certificate, bridge damping plus tail, or full-object signed range control
  would each close adaptive Branch A under the corresponding Paper-23 scalar
  gate.
- It proves that a lower-floor theorem
  \(\overline\Lambda_{13}^{RPF}\ge M_*\) would falsify adaptive Branch A
  after the positive routes fail.
- It proves the current-corpus gaps
  $$
  \begin{gathered}
  \mathrm{P30\text{-}SIGNED\text{-}BRIDGE\text{-}DIRECT\text{-}GAP},\\
  \mathrm{P30\text{-}SIGNED\text{-}BRIDGE\text{-}DUAL\text{-}GAP},\\
  \mathrm{P30\text{-}BRIDGEDAMP\text{-}TAIL\text{-}GAP},\\
  \mathrm{P30\text{-}SIGNED\text{-}FULL\text{-}GAP},\\
  \mathrm{P30\text{-}SIGNED\text{-}BRIDGE\text{-}FLOOR\text{-}GAP},\\
  \mathrm{P30\text{-}SIGNED\text{-}BRIDGE\text{-}LABEL\text{-}NOGO}.
  \end{gathered}
  $$
- It closes the signed/bridge audit at the current-corpus level: more
  finite labels do not move the proof unless they carry new same-law values.
- It then opens the first analytic unblock route rather than another label
  audit.  It proves `P30-PARENT-PUSH-DOM`: scalar conditional variation is
  bounded by parent finite-gauge conditional variation after deterministic
  pushforward.
- It proves `P30-PARENT-LOGOSC-DOM`: parent pointwise log-cross-ratio bounds
  descend to scalar log-Hamiltonian mixed oscillation bounds under the scalar
  pushforward.
- It proves `P30-FV-DLR-EXACT`: the scalar bridge conditional is the
  pushforward/mix of the exact finite-volume parent DLR conditional in a
  tree-gauge chart.
- It defines the effective bridge heat-time slope \(\tau_{br}^{cof}\), the
  residual tilt slope \(\chi_{tilt}^{cof}\), and bridge entropy \(g_{br}\).
  The analytic closure test is
  $$
  {1\over2}C_{min}^{br}\tau_{br}^{cof}
  -
  \chi_{tilt}^{cof}
  >
  g_{br},
  $$
  followed by the Paper-23 bridge margin and the common tail source.
- It proves that this would source bridge damping, but records the
  current-corpus gaps `P30-TREE-HK-BRIDGEDAMP-GAP` and
  `P30-TREE-HK-SIGNED-GAP`.
- It then freezes the bridge-exponent worksheet.  The heat-kernel part is
  controlled by the cofinal slope \(\tau_{br}^{cof}\); the Casimir account
  is a representation-theoretic floor once `P30-CASIMIR-NORM(lambda_HK)` is
  fixed; the entropy account reduces to
  `P30-BRIDGE-ENTROPY-TABLE(M_type,Delta_br)`; and normalizer tilt is
  controlled by primitive potential oscillation.
- It proves the four-account closure theorem:
  $$
  {1\over2}C_0\tau_0-\chi_0>\log(M_{type}\Delta_{br})
  $$
  plus the Paper-23 tail margin sources the bridge-damping route.
- It records the active Part-III front as
  `P30-BRIDGE-TIME-SLOPE-GAP`, `P30-TILT-RPF-GAP`, and
  `P30-BRIDGE-ENTROPY-TABLE-GAP`.  More finite labels cannot solve the first
  two; the entropy table is useful only because it states the exact price
  the same-law analytic value theorem must beat.
- It executes the finite account pass: `P30-CASIMIR-NORM(1)` is closed in the
  Paper-20 standard heat-kernel normalization, true bridges pay at least the
  fundamental Casimir floor, and the complete over-refined Paper-21/Paper-23
  carrier gives
  $$
  g_{br}\le g_{br}^{99},\qquad \log g_{br}^{99}\le157.02.
  $$
  This proves a valid coarse entropy certificate but leaves
  `P30-BRIDGE-ENTROPY-SHARP-GAP` if a useful physical selector is needed.
- It executes the time-slope unit audit.  With carrier-size bridge length,
  the finite `SEL2` sheet-time window forces
  \(\tau_{br}^{cof}(\ell_{car})=0\) whenever bridge lengths are unbounded.
  Thus a positive heat-kernel bridge exponent must use a time-compatible
  bridge length and pay entropy in that same unit.  The corrected source is
  `P30-BRIDGE-TIMEENT(g_time)` together with residual tilt control, later
  refined to `P30-TILT-LOCAL-BRIDGE(chi_0)`.
- It executes the Casimir-time salvage audit.  Fixed \(SU(N_0)\), including
  fixed \(N_0=4096\), cannot rescue carrier-size damping through the Casimir
  factor.  A carrier-step Casimir-time rescue requires a joint
  \(N(j)\)-with-cutoff branch satisfying \(\liminf_jN(j)/H_j>0\), which must
  be declared as a different large-\(N\) diagnostic rather than a fixed
  continuum Yang-Mills theorem.
- It executes the residual tilt localization audit.  Endpoint-additive,
  endpoint-blind, normalizer, heat-time tangent, and HKSD interior tangent
  terms do not charge the doubly centered bridge tilt.  The only remaining
  positive source in this route is
  `P30-TILT-LOCAL-BRIDGE(chi_0)`, i.e. same-law control of the real 4D
  off-sheet/Bianchi/RN mixed residual term.
- It then sharpens the residual-defect question itself.  The exact bound is
  `P30-BRIDGE-INV-XRATIO(C,Omega,kappa)`, which closes the signed route when
  \(2C+\Omega^2/4<M_{\mathrm{sgn}}(\kappa)\).  Paper 30 proves three
  same-law sufficient ways to source it: a maximal involution-defect KP
  theorem, an involution-defect Dobrushin/activity theorem, or a projected
  low-mode plus tail theorem.  The opposite negative route is the
  sign-coherent involution-defect witness, hence the lower floor.
- It records the current-corpus gaps
  `P30-BRIDGE-INV-DEFECT-DOB-GAP`,
  `P30-BRIDGE-INV-LOWTAIL-GAP`, and
  `P30-BRIDGE-INV-DEFECT-WIT-GAP`: Papers 20--30 do not print the needed
  actual defect conditional influence/activity, projected defect matrix and
  tail, or sign-coherent lower-floor witness.
- It completes the prove/falsify pass for the three positive source routes.
  Maximal-defect KP, involution-defect Dobrushin/activity, and projected
  low-mode plus tail are all conditionally sufficient, all not proved by the
  current corpus, and all falsified as current-corpus derivations by
  same-record residual-tail completions.  None is globally falsified as a
  possible future theorem about the actual adaptive law.
- It then defines the Branch-A-only overcoming packages:
  `P30-BRANCHA-KP-ANCHOR`, `P30-BRANCHA-DOB-ANCHOR`, and
  `P30-BRANCHA-LOWTAIL-ANCHOR`.  These are actual-law value anchors for,
  respectively, connected defect activities, defect conditional
  influence/activity, and projected low-mode plus Peter-Weyl complement.
  Each anchor defeats the corresponding residual-tail non-derivability
  argument and closes Branch A if its margin inequality is satisfied.
- It then audits the anchor values themselves.  Paper 30 proves that the
  anchor values are not proven, not falsified, and not decidable from the
  current corpus: pass-like and fail-like same-record completions preserve
  all printed closed ledgers.  A real proof or falsification of the anchor
  values requires new actual finite-volume conditional data or an equivalent
  same-law analytic theorem.
- It then finds the first new same-law quantitative information available
  from the actual finite-volume law: finite-DLR range and boundary log-ratio
  envelopes.  These print the actual same-law quantities
  \(\Delta_{xy}^{DLR,N,j}\), the Dobrushin envelope
  \(\sum_y e^{ad(x,y)}\tanh(\Delta_{xy}^{DLR,N,j}/4)\), the Möbius range
  envelope for defect activities, and the exact projected Peter-Weyl
  low-mode/tail quantities for the bridge defect.
- It proves the honest non-closing verdict for this first extractor.  Crude
  finite-DLR range control is finite at fixed regulator but does not close
  Branch A cofinally: heat-kernel range diverges as small sheet time tends to
  zero, the Dobrushin \(\tanh\)-bound saturates, and pure range information
  gives no Peter-Weyl coefficient decay.
- It therefore turns the vague demand for "new same-law information" into
  three concrete next analytic targets: cancellation/cluster improvement in
  the Möbius activity envelope, a genuinely small DLR boundary log-ratio row,
  or same-law Peter-Weyl coefficient decay for the residual defect.
- It then performs a radical same-law search pass.  The explored routes are
  score/covariance response, connected Möbius/cumulant cancellation,
  heat-kernel Peter-Weyl smoothing plus residual tail, finite
  Schwinger-Dyson/Ward signed bridge identities, transport or entropic
  contraction, and the lower-floor exit.
- For each route it proves the finite same-law identity or conditional
  closure implication actually available, then proves the current-corpus
  non-sourcing verdict.  The resulting live theorem list is
  `P30-CONN-MOBIUS`, `P30-SCORE-COV-ROW`,
  `P30-HK-RESID-PWTAIL`, `P30-WARD-BRIDGE`, and
  `P30-RADICAL-FLOOR`.
- It then goes beyond the non-sourcing ledger by rewriting the exact finite
  parent DLR conditional as a same-law Peter-Weyl representation-history
  sum.  This proves the spin-foam DLR formula, a flux-selection rule for
  projected bridge coefficients, and a foam-tail bound for the omitted
  Peter-Weyl complement.
- The new constructive frontier is `P30-SPINFOAM-TAIL(r_L)`: prove that the
  high-charge representation-history tail is below the Paper-30 low-mode/tail
  margin, preferably through a high-charge area lower bound, residual
  insertion decay, signed/intertwiner cancellation, and a denominator lower
  bound.
- It then formulates the sharper nonabelian switching program.  Corridor
  recouplings are legal same-law maps of representation histories, but exact
  Ising-style switching is not automatic because amplitudes include
  nonabelian recoupling phases and the actual RPF/Jacobian residual
  insertion.
- The live switching theorem is
  `P30-NONABELIAN-SWITCHING(delta,u)`.  Its primitive subgates are
  `P30-SWITCH-RESID-QI`, `P30-SWITCH-NEUTRAL`, and
  `P30-SWITCH-UNPAIRED`, with `P30-SWITCH-AREA` proposed as the way to pay
  the unpaired sector.
- It then runs the minimal-corridor amplitude-ratio audit.  The exact
  termwise ratio factors as \(R_{HK}R_F R_{RPF}\), and termwise neutrality is
  not generic.  The correct replacement is block switching: use the finite
  recoupling matrix \(U_{\Gamma_1}\), the signed insertion matrix
  \(\Sigma_{\Gamma_1}\), the heat-kernel diagonal matrix
  \(D_{\Gamma_1}^{HK}\), and the residual matrix \(\mathcal R_{\Gamma_1}\).
- The new concrete switching target is `P30-BLOCK-SWITCH(theta,u)`, i.e. a
  same-law finite trace-norm bound for
  \(D^{HK}\mathcal R\Sigma+U^*D^{HK}\mathcal R\Sigma U\) plus the unblocked
  sector debit.
- It then prints the universal \(F\otimes F^*\) block table:
  \(U_N=\begin{pmatrix}1/N&\sqrt{N^2-1}/N\\
  \sqrt{N^2-1}/N&-1/N\end{pmatrix}\) and
  \(D^{HK}=\operatorname{diag}(1,(N^2-1)e^{-t_p\lambda_{HK}N})\).  The
  optimistic switch-odd insertion still leaks by
  \(|h_0-h_A|\sqrt{N^2-1}/N\) when the residual is scalar, so the sharp
  subgate is `P30-BLOCK-EVEN-SMALL(theta)`.

## V3 Paper 31: Same-Law Source-Response Calculus

Suggested title:

`Same-Law Source-Response Calculus And Curvature Campaign`

Draft:

`relativistic-isp-v3-paper31-same-law-source-response-calculus.md`

Current status:

- Paper 31 is the continuation forced by the Paper-30 source-response
  reframing.  It is not a synthesis paper, and it is now finished as a
  calculus.
- It keeps the Barandes-aligned same-law rule: all derivatives are
  derivatives of deterministic finite source insertions evaluated at zero
  under the actual adaptive finite DLR law.  No hidden Markov process, no
  auxiliary heat-kernel measure, and no substitute Yang-Mills law is
  introduced.
- It defines a general finite source pressure
  \(\Psi_Q(s)=\log \mathbf E^{act}[\exp(sV_Q)]\), plus multi-source
  pressures \(\Psi(\mathbf s)\).
- It gives a derivative dictionary:
  first derivatives are values, second derivatives are covariances,
  mixed boundary/interior derivatives are influence rows, higher centered
  derivatives are connected/Mobius activities, trace-dual suprema are
  norm debits, and sign-coherent source slopes are floor witnesses.
- It exports this dictionary to the active obstructions:
  Paper-30 heat-bad weighted defect, Paper-29 low-mode entries,
  RN-MIXAMP mixed rows, primitive residual atoms, Dobrushin rows,
  defect KP/Mobius activities, bridge residual tilt, and Peter-Weyl tail
  gates.
- Its closure theorem is that source-response is complete and non-closing:
  every opened obstruction has an exact derivative representation, but
  smallness, tail decay, nonlinear Dobrushin contraction, and floors still
  require primitive same-law analytic inputs.
- The next live targets are no longer further source rearrangements but one
  of the primitive inputs: heat-bad source neutrality/curvature, low-mode
  source response gap, mixed RN-MIXAMP Ward/curvature control, nonlinear
  source-Dobrushin upgrade, connected source-cumulant decay, same-law
  Peter-Weyl regularity/tail, or sign-coherent lower floor.

Executed work packages:

1. **Define the source-response calculus.** Freeze same-law finite source
   pressures, first response, curvature, mixed response, and higher
   cumulant derivatives: completed.
2. **Print the derivative dictionary.** Classify all relevant derivatives
   and norm duals that can replace missing row-value tables: completed.
3. **Export to Paper-30 heat-bad.** Recast the heat-bad matrix as the first
   worked source-response target: completed.
4. **Export to Paper-29/Paper-28 spectral gates.** Recast low-mode entries,
   strict spectral gap, and Peter-Weyl tail as source-response objects:
   completed.
5. **Export to RN-MIXAMP/Dobrushin/KP/floor gates.** Recast mixed RN rows,
   influence rows, connected activities, and lower floors as derivatives:
   completed.
6. **Close the source-response menu.** Prove the identity-level calculus,
   prove no-free-smallness, audit heat-bad, low-mode, RN-MIXAMP, primitive
   atom, Dobrushin, KP/Mobius, Peter-Weyl, and floor routes, and record each
   as proved identity, conditionally reduced primitive, or current-corpus
   non-derivation: completed.

## V3 Paper 32: Heat-Bad Source Neutrality, Curvature, Or Floor

Suggested title:

`Heat-Bad Source Neutrality, Curvature, Or Floor`

Draft:

`relativistic-isp-v3-paper32-heat-bad-source-neutrality-curvature-or-floor.md`

Current status:

- Paper 32 is the direct attack on the first primitive input selected after
  Paper 31.  It is not a summary and it does not introduce a comparison law.
- It keeps the Barandes-aligned same-law rule: the source parameter is only a
  deterministic finite generating parameter, all claims are derivatives or
  finite pressure identities at \(s=0\) under the actual adaptive law, and no
  hidden Markov process or substitute heat-kernel measure is introduced.
- The central viewpoint shift is switch-pressure rather than matrix-entry
  recovery.  For each heat-bad dual source \(Q\), the source observable is
  split as \(V_Q=V_Q^{odd}+V_Q^{even}\) under the Paper-30 recoupling switch.
- Paper 32 proves that, under a same-law switch symmetry, exact switch-odd
  sources have exactly even pressure, and a bounded switch-even defect gives
  source neutrality:
  $$
  |\Psi_Q(a)-\Psi_Q(-a)|
  \le 2a\|V_Q^{even}\|_\infty.
  $$
- Hence `P32-HKBAD-EVENDEF(epsilon)` implies
  `P32-HKBAD-SRC-NEUT(a,a epsilon)`, and together with
  `P32-HKBAD-SRC-CURV(a,chi)` gives the heat-bad debit
  $$
  \epsilon+{\chi a\over2}.
  $$
- It then audits every route to the curvature or floor constant: universal
  oscillation, source Poincare/log-Sobolev, Ward-Stein inversion,
  Peter-Weyl low/tail regularity, direct response, and sign-coherent lower
  floor.
- Its second pass replaces the too-strong exact switch-law assumption by a
  finite switch quasi-invariance gate `P32-HKBAD-SWQI(omega)`.  With switch
  RN oscillation \(\omega\), the closing debit becomes
  \(\epsilon+\omega/(2a)+\chi a/2\), optimized to
  \(\epsilon+\sqrt{\omega\chi}\).
- It prints the exact heat-bad three-term decomposition into weighted signed
  parity, residual/Jacobian switch defect, and heat-bad product term.  The
  product-thinness gate `P32-HKBAD-PRODTHIN(tau)` is now the sharpest
  pointwise route to the even-defect bound; the weaker
  `P32-HKBAD-EVENRESP(epsilon)` is the response-only fallback.
- It then attacks those gates: `P32-HKBAD-SWQI(omega)` is reduced to the
  finite DLR switch-Hamiltonian oscillation
  \(\Omega_{SW}^{DLR,N,j}(B_{HB})\); product thinness is compared two-sidedly
  with the heat-bad product term under heat-mismatch nondegeneracy; and
  `P32-HKBAD-PRODFLOOR(M)` is printed as the negative sign-coherent fork.
- Its trap audit proves that small residual/Jacobian switch variation cannot
  source `SWQI` on a heat-bad component with a positive heat switch floor.
  The needed positive theorem is residual/Jacobian counter-tilt
  `P32-HKBAD-SWCOUNTER(omega)`, not residual neutrality.
- It also splits product thinness into nondegenerate product control plus
  null-sector product mass, and isolates `P32-HKBAD-EVEN-WARD(kappa)` as the
  minimal Ward/Stein route to even-response smallness.
- Its anti-heat pass rewrites `P32-HKBAD-SWCOUNTER(omega)` as
  `P32-HKBAD-ANTIHEAT-ATOM(omega)`: a switched residual Möbius-atom sum must
  cancel the heat switch mismatch modulo constants.  It proves that small
  residual switch atoms leave the heat floor exposed, and that the positive
  route really needs `P32-HKBAD-CT-PROD-COMP(omega,tau)`, compatibility
  between anti-heat counter-tilt and product thinness on the same actual
  residual atom family.
- Its compatibility-geometry pass turns that condition into the finite
  quotient-distance problem \(d_{prod}^{N,j}(\omega)\le\tau\): the anti-heat
  target class must lie near the product-null/product-small cone.  If the
  heat target is product-visible and sign-coherent, the route turns into the
  floor fork.
- Its certificate pass turns the quotient-distance problem into a finite
  convex program.  Positive closure is witnessed by
  `P32-HKBAD-QDIST-UP(omega,tau,L,delta)`, an explicit anti-heat field plus
  trace-norm dilation certificate.  Negative closure is witnessed by
  `P32-HKBAD-QDIST-DUAL-FLOOR(M,L,delta)`, a dual product functional that
  sees the heat target and is sign-coherent in the Branch-A ledger.
- Its rowprint pass proves that the structural entries demanded by
  Corollary 38.2 are sourced, but the actual heat-bad product columns
  \(A_\Gamma^{N,j,L}\) are not.  It defines
  `P32-HKBAD-PRODENTRY(L,epsilon_data)` and then sharpens the preferred
  positive theorem to the narrower quotient-response source
  `P32-HKBAD-QRESP(L,epsilon_data)`.
- Its polar-response pass attacks `QRESP`: it defines the finite certificate
  polar family, proves the polar first-response identity, and reduces the
  route to `P32-HKBAD-QPOLAR-SWODD + P32-HKBAD-QPOLAR-CURV`, or to
  `P32-HKBAD-QPOLAR-WARD`, with `P32-HKBAD-QPOLAR-FLOOR` as the negative
  route.
- Its three-route pass explores those polar alternatives: switch-odd plus
  curvature, polar Ward/Stein, and polar floor.  Each is valid as a finite
  same-law theorem, but each requires a new instantiated polar table or
  actual-law Ward/floor witness not printed by the current corpus.
- Its minimal worksheet pass instantiates the Paper-30 singlet-adjoint
  crossing block.  The known structural entries are \(U_N\),
  \(D_{\Gamma_1}^{HK}\), and the heat-bad classification; all three routes
  reduce to the actual \(2\times2\) same-law product
  \(B_{\Gamma_1}^{N,j}=R_{\Gamma_1}^{N,j}\Sigma_{\Gamma_1}^{N,j}\), or
  equivalently to its finite polar responses.
- Its explicit-algebra pass compresses the product table further.  The
  minimal polar defect is exactly \((mI_2+tU_N)/2\), where
  \(m=h_0\beta_{00}+h_A\beta_{AA}\) and
  \(t=a_N(h_0\beta_{00}-h_A\beta_{AA})+
  b_N(h_0\beta_{0A}+h_A\beta_{A0})\).  Thus the live value theorem is the
  two-scalar table `P32-HKBAD-MINPOL-MTABLE`, with smallness, Ward, or floor
  exits.
- Its two-scalar attack defines the same-law pressure \(\Psi_{MT}^{N,j}\),
  proves the first-response identities for \(m,t\), proves the centering
  involution implication with controlled log-RN defect, and then rules out
  the available structural centerings: crossing fixes \(m,t\), gauge/Haar
  Ward identities leave scalar intertwiners free, and selector relabeling is
  tautological unless it changes the actual numerical block product.  The
  floor candidates are exactly \(m,t,\lambda_+,\lambda_-\), with
  \(\lambda_\pm=(m\pm t)/2\).
- Its Peter-Weyl continuation defines the common same-law tail theorem
  `P32-SLAW-PWTAIL`, proves Sobolev and analytic sufficient criteria,
  identifies residual multiplier tameness as the only plausible way to
  transfer clean heat-kernel damping to actual residual observables, and
  proves that heat-kernel smoothness alone does not control residual
  Hamiltonians, Jacobians, conditional ratios, selectors, logarithms, or
  residual-score derivatives.
- Its six-gate transfer pass proves the conditional package
  `P32-SLAW-PW-XFER` and audits each required gate: Sobolev derivative
  bounds, residual multiplier tameness, normalizer lower bounds, projection
  commutator decay, residual-score regularity, and high-mode floor.  All six
  are valid primitive targets, and none is sourced by the current corpus.
- Its local source-Dobrushin pass defines the live observable family
  \({\mathcal O}_{live}^{N,j}\), finite boundary source family
  \({\mathcal B}_{bd}^{N,j}\), mixed source pressure, linear and nonlinear
  influence rows, and the local theorem `P32-SRC-DOB-LOCAL(q,a)`.  It proves
  the conditional Neumann bound for \(q<1\), proves the linear-plus-curvature
  upgrade to a finite nonlinear row, audits the finite-DLR log-ratio envelope,
  and prints `P32-SRC-DOB-FLOOR(M_*)` as the negative alternative.  The local
  Dobrushin route is valid, but still requires new actual-law source
  response, curvature, DLR-envelope, or floor information.
- Its mixed RN-MIXAMP Ward/curvature pass imports the Paper-27 weighted row,
  defines the residual-tilted mixed source pressure, proves endpoint-additive
  cancellation, prints the finite same-law Ward identity
  \(\mathbf E[XF]=\mathbf E[FS_X]\), and proves two conditional positive
  exits: Ward span plus Ward-score defect control, or Ward base control plus
  residual-tilt curvature.  It identifies the curvature as a connected third
  source cumulant, proves that gauge/Haar Ward identities alone do not source
  the needed mixed scalar row, and prints the sign-coherent mixed Ward floor
  as the negative route.
- Its connected source-cumulant pass defines the retained defect/Mobius
  source family, the connected source cumulants, and the KP-weighted cumulant
  norm.  It proves that `P32-CONN-SRC-KP(q,a)` would source the
  defect-polymer theorem and reopen primitive residual value extraction; it
  records finite projection exports to RN-MIXAMP tilt curvature, local
  source-Dobrushin curvature, and Peter-Weyl score cumulants; and it audits
  why moment-cumulant identities, clean KP estimates, and the defect
  Dobrushin route are not enough in the current corpus.  Its floor fork is
  `P32-CONN-SRC-FLOOR`.
- Its post-menu Ward/Stein range pass records the concrete attack plan:
  convert live values into a finite same-law Ward/Stein range problem, then
  either control the Ward score defect or use the separating dual as a floor
  candidate.  It defines the joint live quotient, actual Ward/Stein module,
  target span, range distance, score-defect theorem, and dual certificate. It
  executes the first subtest by proving that the pure gauge/Haar Ward module
  cannot contain \(M,T,\lambda_\pm\) unless those scalar classes are already
  zero.  The remaining positive target is residual/selector range plus
  residual-score defect.
- Its residual/selector execution defines the smallest-block coordinate map
  \(\Phi_{\Gamma_1}^{N,j,L}\), residual Jacobian \(J_{res}^{N,j,L}\),
  residual range gate, and residual score-defect gate.  It proves that
  selector-only label directions have zero live Jacobian, so only numerical
  residual/selector motion can move the live obstruction.  It proves the
  conditional closure from residual range plus residual score-defect, and
  records the dual floor alternative when the rank gate fails.
- Its five-step residual-range worksheet instantiates the smallest block-entry
  chart, prints the scalar target map, and proves that \(m,t,\lambda_+,
  \lambda_-\) have only two independent scalar directions.  Hence the scalar
  rank side passes in the block-entry envelope.  The unsourced positive
  inputs are now the actual admissibility of those block-entry vector fields,
  the RN block-derivative table `P32-RN-BLKDER(L)`, and the scalar residual
  score-defect estimate `P32-SCAL-RESDEFECT(delta)`.
- Its finite RN derivative attack proves that `P32-RN-BLKDER(L)` is not a
  primitive table until a lift/factorization gate is sourced.  The exact new
  finite fork is `P32-BLKFIELD-ADM + P32-RN-BETA-FACTOR`, which makes
  \(K_{RN}^{blk}=D_\theta W_{RN}R_{blk}\) canonical, or
  `P32-RN-KERSEP`, which proves the four-entry block envelope is too small
  and sends the rank problem back to the full residual Jacobian.
- Its scalar-admissibility refinement proves that the minimal scalar
  heat-bad route should not pay for the full four-entry block lift.  The
  scalar route needs only `P32-SCALFIELD-ADM`, sourced by either
  `P32-SCAL-CONFJAC` or `P32-SCAL-SRCMAT`, plus the existing
  `P32-SCAL-RESDEFECT(delta)`.
- Its configuration-Jacobian attack proves that `P32-SCAL-CONFJAC` is not
  sourced unless one prints a same-law pointwise lift of \(m,t\).  Atom-value
  and group-coordinate lifts are not printed, and free coordinates are not
  same-law observables.  The positive scalar branch is now
  `P32-SCAL-SRC-RANK + P32-SCAL-SRC-CURV + P32-SCAL-RESDEFECT`.
- Its source-rank worksheet proves that `P32-SCAL-SRC-RANK` is a finite
  determinant-minor problem.  The exact positive gate is
  `P32-SCAL-SRC-DET(A,B;Delta,M_C)`.  The exact negative gate is
  `P32-SCAL-SRC-RANK-GAP` plus a sign-coherent scalar floor.  The current
  corpus prints neither.
- Its structural source tomography pass defines the two-knob source
  \(S_{\alpha,\zeta}\), structural pressure \(\Phi_{str}\), realization gate
  `P32-SCAL-STRUCTSRC-ID`, Gram gate `P32-SCAL-STRUCTSRC-GRAM`, and
  rigidity/floor exit.  It proves that realized structural sources plus Gram
  positivity would source scalar rank, but clean structural knobs alone do
  not couple to the actual residual/signed product.  The compact positive
  scalar target is now
  `P32-SCAL-STRUCTSRC-COUPLE + P32-SCAL-STRUCTSRC-GRAM`.
- The closure theorem is honest: Paper 32 proves the sharp reduction and
  fully identifies the primitive missing inputs.  The missing object is now
  the minimal scalar actual-law table `P32-HKBAD-MINPOL-MTABLE`, a new
  non-gauge Ward/centering theorem for \(m,t\), or a sign-coherent floor
  witness for \(m,t,\lambda_+,\lambda_-\); or, on the tail side, actual
  Sobolev/analytic regularity, multiplier tameness, normalizer lower bounds,
  commutator decay, score regularity, or a high-mode sign-coherent floor; or,
  on the local-Dobrushin side, a strict same-law source-Dobrushin row, a
  linear row plus curvature upgrade, a closing DLR log-ratio envelope, or a
  local source-Dobrushin floor; or, on the mixed RN-MIXAMP side, Ward span
  plus Ward-defect control, Ward-base plus residual-tilt curvature, or a
  sign-coherent mixed Ward floor; or, on the connected-cumulant side, a
  strict defect source-KP theorem, projection constants exporting it to other
  routes, or a sign-coherent connected cumulant floor; or, on the post-menu
  joint range side, residual/selector Ward/Stein range, residual score-defect
  control, or a joint separating dual floor.
